
-----title
金华 (出生地)

DetailSwitch("c83e7756e4f04b1b870ce7848f46a79d");'><span id='c83e7756e4f04b1b870ce7848f46a79d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　刚中父郑卞于此年由醴陵令致仕，携家眷归东阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年11月4日</a>　刚中父卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1111')">1106-1111年</a>　郑刚中居金华家乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　为乡贡首。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='608d57af5da3448793f1dc78c016ff5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("608d57af5da3448793f1dc78c016ff5e");'><span id='608d57af5da3448793f1dc78c016ff5e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1120')">1114-1120年</a>，27-33岁</div><div id='608d57af5da3448793f1dc78c016ff5e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1116')">1114-1116年</a>　疑居家乡待荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　郑刚中拜天台左先生于金华。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　郑母盛氏夫人终天。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1119')">1118-1119年</a>　疑居家乡待荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　母盛氏夫人归葬。作品：《谢梅右司作先夫人埋铭书》《谢宇文郎中书先夫人埋铭书》<div id='poem_1234359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢梅右司作先夫人埋铭书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234359")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234359'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234359'>某闻玉出昆崙，流沙万里之外，经千译乃至中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234359_comment'></div>有文章于此，与美玉同，而其来之远，则有类于流沙千译之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234359_comment'></div>某方语人曰「我欲得此」，则人信之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234359_comment'></div>必不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234359_comment'></div>金矿于山，篝火糇粮而后进，崖崩窟塞，则取者遂葬其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234359_comment'></div>有文章于此，与良金同，而其得之难，则又不啻有崖窟覆压之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234359_comment'></div>某方语人曰「我欲得此」，则人信之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234359_comment'></div>必不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234359_comment'></div>某前年失母氏，昏迷中但念罪逆重大，无消除之理，懿行隐没，无发扬之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234359_comment'></div>故不避僭冒，以志铭血恳，上及座下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234359_comment'></div>当是时，正犹越流沙而求玉，探深凿而取金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234359_comment'></div>其高下隔阔，内负惕息之状，固有倍万于金玉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234359_comment'></div>是故无亲疏之愚，皆谓某不善量度，无可得之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234359_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234359_comment'></div>某至穷贱者也，公当今贵人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234359_comment'></div>分既不相及，东西数千里，情亦不相通，安可投置番纸短书于潭潭之府，遂欲得其无价文章？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234359_comment'></div>又况旌人遗德，刻之金石，所以垂信后世，其事甚重，其不可得固无疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234359_comment'></div>独某狂妄之心，谓公殖学播名，正跻显道，方欲镇压偷俗，激扬义风，其于葭莩旧属，瓜葛遗情，当未泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234359_comment'></div>是以无昼夜延颈西望，定期蝼蚁之诚有所感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234359_comment'></div>果以八月十三日奉教书，悉遂所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234359_comment'></div>沾濡膏馥，不但枉勤大笔，而古篆小楷，皆得显者为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234359_comment'></div>披卷发函，烂烂在目，徬徨感激，涕泪迸流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234359_comment'></div>再拜叩头，移入翠石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234359_comment'></div>竁兆既启，谨已锁置幽堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234359_comment'></div>而妙刻流传，今亦不可以数计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234359_comment'></div>此皆右司德厚仁深，情坚义重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234359_comment'></div>念昔时齐眉庑下之贤，故以某母氏为可录；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234359_comment'></div>享今日戏䌽高堂之乐，故以某孤苦为堪伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234359_comment'></div>不靳毫芒，勒为藏史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234359_comment'></div>流芳托此，遂播无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234359_comment'></div>呜呼，岂不谓之厚恩也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234359_comment'></div>是小人忘生杀身之地，刳肠奉首之报，今得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234359_comment'></div>昔杜舍人尝谓自古言恳者莫若申包胥求救于秦，以其七日七夜哭声不绝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234359_comment'></div>言喜者莫若虢国太子，以其死而复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234359_comment'></div>某曩为母氏乞铭时，正类包胥之恳，非不哭也，第公不闻其哭尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234359_comment'></div>今此过蒙恩悯，充足所愿，且得于忧患祸灾之馀，付以辉光，是亦死而复生者，其为喜也不减虢国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1234359_comment'></div>谨以石刻一本，随此封献，少通谢意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1234359_comment'></div>辞语烦碎，不胜惶惧流汗之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1234359_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234360' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234360' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234360?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢宇文郎中书先夫人埋铭书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234360")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234360_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234360'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234360'>某嗜古读书，窃有恶圆之僻，每见传记间有立身谨严、行事端正者，则倾心慕望，恨不可一见如天神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234360_comment'></div>其后有教某者曰：「子云有言：书，心画也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234360_comment'></div>公权亦谓心正则笔正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234360_comment'></div>欲察昔人贤否，第于今石刻间视其笔法行动，则忠佞邪正，一眄可得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234360_comment'></div>某审其言，似或可用，凡残碑旧字，皆收拾验视，参合其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234360_comment'></div>又见如鲁公辈勒名著行，皎如星日，而字画之存者，坚刚方正，严毅整肃，定无零乱妩媚之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234360_comment'></div>自是始信教者为不谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234360_comment'></div>每欲挟此术以观当世贵人，则廊庙馆阁之间，端人正士既非穷贱寒生所及识，而又翰墨尊贵，秘藏难得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234360_comment'></div>脱或挥洒到人间，则又非穷贱寒生之所可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234360_comment'></div>故孤怀常抱慕望不足之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234360_comment'></div>前年失母氏，冒祸毒，丐铭于右司梅公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234360_comment'></div>公视某之父，则昔之僚婿也，怜而与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234360_comment'></div>且赐某书曰：「吾既为汝铭其母，又得宇文公书之，无忽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234360_comment'></div>某踊跃再拜，既感母氏有没后之光如此，窃自庆幸于今日得见当世贵人之书，可以验信其术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234360_comment'></div>聚族共观之，则满纸灿烂，皆持重舒和，遒峻紧结，无点画不有法度，而终不为边幅所窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234360_comment'></div>正如冠剑大臣俨立于朝堂之上，风采威仪，自有贵气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234360_comment'></div>呜呼，诚无价之宝也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234360_comment'></div>顾贤杰之士，志业超爽，岂尝留情小艺，乃其忠纯温厚之气根著于心，故发挥于外者自然如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234360_comment'></div>恭惟郎中力正学而收峻科，行直道而领要职，蕴藉风流，标致高远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234360_comment'></div>在搢绅间沈邃有韵，故字画锋力俱全，不蹈前迹，挺挺奇伟，非苟然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234360_comment'></div>观人之术，真可验矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234360_comment'></div>某东浙书生，藉箕裘之业，免为聋瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234360_comment'></div>然自幼时所受者，皆穷苦顿挫之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234360_comment'></div>已三十年虚为太平男子，众方指为沟中穷人，一旦乃能为母氏得柳书，遂与唐人子孙争孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234360_comment'></div>吁，可怪哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234360_comment'></div>自非阁下与右司公雅相交厚，不忍其乡里姻戚中辄有栖栖抱苦者，则此等字画，正为神佛护持，岂在寒家墓石上耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234360_comment'></div>人非木土，安得无知！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234360_comment'></div>衔荷厚恩，死而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234360_comment'></div>于今而后，所谓立身谨严，行事端正者，又何必远慕古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234360_comment'></div>如或终坐坎𡒄，不得见馀尘而一拜，则松楸之下，高悬妙刻，自可终此身而仰事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234360_comment'></div>不胜拳拳之至，谨以母氏墓志一轴，同此封献，伏幸采目。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1234360_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='aca015687e7d40a9a76a1b702eb2685d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aca015687e7d40a9a76a1b702eb2685d");'><span id='aca015687e7d40a9a76a1b702eb2685d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1126')">1123-1126年</a>，36-39岁</div><div id='aca015687e7d40a9a76a1b702eb2685d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　族兄宗鲁母侯夫人归葬。作品：《代族兄宗鲁作母侯夫人行状》<div id='poem_1234680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代族兄宗鲁作母侯夫人行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234680")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234680'>吾母族裔，皆舅氏所详，洙不敢具，谨约其节行之实，泣血而叙之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234680_comment'></div>母氏年十又七归郑氏，归四十年而寡，寡二十二年，以宣和庚子某月日终，以癸卯某月日葬于东阳乡保福原，祔吾父司录公之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234680_comment'></div>男三人，女三人，孙男十一人，孙女八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234680_comment'></div>此其大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234680_comment'></div>吾祖中散多男子，夫人在诸妇间，孝谨有特誉，不忤妯娌之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234680_comment'></div>司录公虽入仕，雅意不在富贵，日以诗酒宾客为乐，夫人周旋承顺，以廉谨相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234680_comment'></div>历四任而洙孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234680_comment'></div>洙自念发齿踰壮，不自冲跃，今无以奉事吾母，因与兄浚弃置笔砚，共力丘园，生事稍给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234680_comment'></div>夫人无累，则诵佛书，不荤茹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234680_comment'></div>赒赈贫乏，宗族之有疾病者，无亲疏大小，治疗皆如己子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234680_comment'></div>见人有过，委曲规切之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234680_comment'></div>闻其有善，则乐为道说之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234680_comment'></div>岁四时庙享，肴醴不自其手出，不敢以祭，老而益严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234680_comment'></div>年来略铅黛，疏绮帛，雍容康宁，而门户整肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234680_comment'></div>下迨诸孙、孙妇，辑睦和洽，无一人敢立礼法之外，夫人怡怡笑语而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234680_comment'></div>给事刘公为贺之明年，夫人年七十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234680_comment'></div>刘公视侯氏为姻家，登堂上寿，而远近亲族以宝货币帛为礼者，不知其计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234680_comment'></div>夫人谨不敢受，谓洙等曰：「吾今日得孙子诜诜，坐受安乐，正宜归庆于汝之祖父，是礼非吾所敢当」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234680_comment'></div>既不得辞，则尽取以散施贫窭，一物不留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234680_comment'></div>捐舍之日，橐中萧然，人皆服其有识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234680_comment'></div>某窃谓此等皆宜为舅氏所书，谨泣血叙次如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234680_comment'></div>谨状<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山文集》卷七。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234680_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1234680'>宗：原无，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1234680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　发两浙漕司荐。作品：《谢漕司秋举启》<div id='poem_1234366' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234366' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234366?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢漕司秋举启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234366")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234366_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234366'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234366'>合三路之秀，谩尔随群；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234366_comment'></div>较一日之长，适然居上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234366_comment'></div>与之偕者踰千辈，出其后者止三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234366_comment'></div>得非所宜，愧亦增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234366_comment'></div>窃以还科举而复熙丰之制，设漕试以防州郡之私，论其为法则岂复有加，所以待士者无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234366_comment'></div>文章丕变，追还浑厚之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234366_comment'></div>场屋一新，革去对偶之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234366_comment'></div>顾常规之稍彻，宜清鉴之无差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234366_comment'></div>如某者江浙孤生，箕裘末系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234366_comment'></div>弟兄终鲜，事朋友则小巫之见，访问儒雅之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234366_comment'></div>矧属古文，暂罹中否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234366_comment'></div>科举乃祖宗之旧，人材皆教化之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234366_comment'></div>不应多故之时，无待价深藏之玉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234366_comment'></div>遂用新科之制，求处囊立见之锥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234366_comment'></div>当得乡贤，使为举首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234366_comment'></div>如某者受才冗恶，赋性疏愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234366_comment'></div>蚤尝踊跃于功名，今渐侵寻于齿发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234366_comment'></div>然愤时振翼，忘其为腹背之毛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234366_comment'></div>顾影长嘶，恨正作缠牵之马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234366_comment'></div>心怀秘计，梦骋良图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234366_comment'></div>旋闻科诏之音，勉作书生之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234366_comment'></div>恋耕锄而首犹躅踯，学诗赋而口尚嗫嚅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234366_comment'></div>忘意桑榆，非缘利禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234366_comment'></div>譬犹滋味，自知咀嚼之迟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234366_comment'></div>徒若秕糠，常在簸飏之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234366_comment'></div>得之增愧，尤所归恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234366_comment'></div>此盖判府给事国士无双，唐朝第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234366_comment'></div>非徒笔语妙天下，盖亦智术过古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234366_comment'></div>留威名于朔廷，布仁恩于辅郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234366_comment'></div>孤城屡寇，指麾才及于期年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234366_comment'></div>万井俱生，全活不知其几口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234366_comment'></div>复引邹生之吹，散为寒谷之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234366_comment'></div>恨借寇之无由，惜丐戎之已晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234366_comment'></div>但坚操节，上报恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234366_comment'></div>庶因堂下之言，可备笼中之药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234366_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1234366_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　刚中得子。作品：《甲辰年得男子经道以诗相贺因报之》<div id='poem_174691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲辰年得男子经道以诗相贺因报之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174691")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174691'>两梦尝占女子祥，偶悬弧矢亦非常。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174691'>渥洼方合生骐骥，枳棘安能出凤凰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174691'>自顾此身无远业，所期前世有遗芳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174691'>新诗相贺来何晚，汤饼惟公不在堂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174691_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年2月</a>　族兄宗鲁去世。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年12月</a>　族兄宗鲁归葬。作品：《族兄宗鲁行状》<div id='poem_1234681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>族兄宗鲁行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234681")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234681'>郑宗鲁，讳洙，字宗鲁，以宣和六年二月甲子卒于里第，享年五十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234681_comment'></div>按其谱，世居婺之金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234681_comment'></div>祖详，以儒学发身，官至中散大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234681_comment'></div>曾祖克从，以中散累赠至金紫光禄大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234681_comment'></div>父汝嘉，以中散任子恩为安州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234681_comment'></div>录事公大姓之后，在官以洁廉自将，不治产，食口众，且好客，而又疏放不事上位，向穷踬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234681_comment'></div>宗鲁告其兄资深曰：「兄弟徒守书卷无益，盍亦归治田园裕我家，使吾父无衣食之累，而益得自遂其志，亦人子一事，书固徐可读也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234681_comment'></div>资深以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234681_comment'></div>宗鲁自是不一志于学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234681_comment'></div>录事公捐舍，哀毁踰制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234681_comment'></div>奉其母侯氏夫人，旨甘惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234681_comment'></div>嫁诸妹与接内外姻族，惟恐不称，故治生愈力，善视丰凶而低昂积散，妙于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234681_comment'></div>数年间，资产大殖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234681_comment'></div>宣和辛丑，睦贼猖炽，所在奔走，蹂躏族属不相收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234681_comment'></div>太夫人年且八十，宗鲁与其妇蒋舁致山间，营营其旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234681_comment'></div>贼执宗鲁而不敢害，卒得护持夫人以寿终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234681_comment'></div>宗鲁既冲冒良苦，且失太夫人，哀忧成疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234681_comment'></div>方即故址建大厦，督工视事，矻矻不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234681_comment'></div>人或勉之曰：「公病矣，何为是苦」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234681_comment'></div>宗鲁曰：「郑自上世，门户蕃大，寇馀无复前人踪迹，吾安忍坐视其凋也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234681_comment'></div>毕力为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234681_comment'></div>落成之后，于其间奉太夫人襄事，迎款宾客，比上世为不衰，人始服其善承家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234681_comment'></div>宗鲁方惩艾厚藏之祸，欲买书教子，益修礼义，力振祖考之遗风，而不幸死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234681_comment'></div>宗鲁为人奇庞厚重，外若雄伟可畏而中实和易，接人熙熙笑语，宗族上下，相得无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234681_comment'></div>六男子：曰瑎、珫、珷、瑶、瑢、瑗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234681_comment'></div>三女子：长适进士侯知彰，次适承务郎刘谠，次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234681_comment'></div>蒋氏先以壬寅八月十四日卒，葬于无相院山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234681_comment'></div>珫泣血来告，将以甲辰十二月庚申，举宗鲁之柩，合于无相山之圹，欲求铭于给事刘公，愿状其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234681_comment'></div>审其行，宜为名卿所书，谨录按如右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234681_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1234681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　疑居家乡待荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年7月7日</a>　疑居家乡待荐。作品：《建炎丁未自中夏徂秋不雨七夕日戏成一诗简牛郎织女云》<div id='poem_174901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建炎丁未自中夏徂秋不雨七夕日戏成一诗简牛郎织女云</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年7月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174901")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174901'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174901'>今夕知何夕，织女逢牵牛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174901'>云軿拥高汉，仙事传风流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174901'>人间适焦窘，龟兆生田畴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174901'>当时大军后，皆抱糠籺忧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174901'>我劝二星者，鹊桥无谩游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174901'>曷不攀天河，驾浪鞭龙头。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174901'>共化油然云，白雨淋九州。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174901_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年9月</a>　刚中小妹亡。作品：《杨氏女弟墓石书丹》<div id='poem_1234685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨氏女弟墓石书丹</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234685")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234685'>兹墓有女，婺州进士杨应梦之孺人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234685_comment'></div>孺人，同郡承事郎郑公讳某之幼女，生于卫之汲县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234685_comment'></div>年七岁，诵书写字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234685_comment'></div>稍长，能属对吟诗，习音乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234685_comment'></div>承事公没，母兄以之归杨氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234685_comment'></div>杨虽大姓，暨孺人归，则其家已凋，产去税在，征求窘切，无以自存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234685_comment'></div>孺人乃略铅黛，躬纺绩，买丝织帛，求羡馀赒一门之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234685_comment'></div>乃夫劳之，则曰：「姑老矣，不如是则君学必废，恐无以称吾姑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234685_comment'></div>如是矻矻劳苦，昼夜不休，竟感疾而卒，建炎丁未八月十七日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234685_comment'></div>呜呼贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234685_comment'></div>孺人享年三十一，男仅五岁，死时就蓐终三日，与所生女婴并亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234685_comment'></div>敛之日，家无馀衣，盖其夫之贫未苏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234685_comment'></div>呜呼痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234685_comment'></div>某，其兄也，既用西方荼毗法哭而火之，而遗孤茕然，念其他日必能寻母之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234685_comment'></div>以其年九月丙申椟其灰而藏诸山，复用柳子厚书砖故事，述其秘行于墓石之盖，以慰杨氏子之心云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234685_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1234685'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234685_comment'></div>夫之贫也如此，未知所立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234685_comment'></div>子之幼也如此，未知所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234685_comment'></div>呜呼，吾妹已矣！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1234685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　疑居家乡待荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　为乡荐首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　疑居家乡待荐。作品：《己酉正月大风寒米价胜踴菜色之民皇皇于道感而作是诗》《己酉立春前一日得雨时有百日之晴》《己酉三月二十一日夜梦中作》《览镜》《与叶彦法》<div id='poem_174675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己酉正月大风寒米价腾踊菜色之民皇皇于道感而作是诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174675")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174675'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174675'>昏昏日影有还无，谩诞春风势力粗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174675'>品物固知春用意，细民其奈米如珠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174675'>未相秦越尝忧国，不再皋夔愧服儒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174675'>骨髓有奇深自负，缄封无路荐区区。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174675'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174675_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174415' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174415' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174415?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己酉立春前一日得雨时有百日之晴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年2月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174415")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174415_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174415'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174415'>阳春明日五更回，破旱先令一雨来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174415'>要得群生蒙实惠，故将膏泽润枯荄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174415_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174415'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174415_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己酉三月二十一日夜梦中作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年3月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174416")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174416'>曲阑干畔短篱边，用意春工剪不圆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174416'>一夜西风借霜力，幽香喷出小金钱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174416'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174416_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>览镜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174930")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174930'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174930'>短发不盈梳，年来半斑白。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174930'>吾今四十二，敢望能满百。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174930'>负郭苦无田，安居未成宅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174930'>况复世路艰，国步日侵迫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174930'>未必松楸旁，常得看书册。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174930'>区区抱短见，贫贱中外隔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174930'>寄此乡国间，踪迹亦如客。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174930'>览镜酒杯空，浩歌天地窄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174930_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174930'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_174930_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与叶彦法</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234391")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234391'>伏自癸卯告别，迨今六年，中间二三书相往复之后，音耗不通矣，怀仰如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234391_comment'></div>即日秋深气爽，福禄骈集，绅笏之荣，实所忻快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234391_comment'></div>异时小人根连党结，欺慢君父，已腼颜受禄，又盗其馀，沾及婚友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234391_comment'></div>市恩之罪，天未显戮，而附炎得志者方沾沾自宠，正如得盗财为盗役，而自以为得志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234391_comment'></div>留守宗丈怀志秉节，于众人忧危撼动之中，忘身勇奋，脱天下生灵之急，传之后世，可以赎今日人材猥敝之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234391_comment'></div>是虽竭美官高爵，未足报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234391_comment'></div>矧坦腹其门、学行兼美如吾友者，受朝廷九品官，不为忝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234391_comment'></div>每欲以数字驰贺，又念前日无书问往来，一旦见人有名称，便奉竿牍，此正世俗之薄习，故因循至今，左右鉴其忠否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234391_comment'></div>前月缘干抵城，似闻里巷有不憖遗之叹，继见宗学士起复之诏，方知果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234391_comment'></div>留守丈晚节腾奋，草木知名，无所愧恨，第可为朝廷惜，不敢为左右及闑内孺人之吊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234391_comment'></div>京畿阙在何时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234391_comment'></div>美赴有日矣否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234391_comment'></div>某穷居如昨，进取事的不在怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234391_comment'></div>但得四野安靖，保守松楸，尽读未见之书，为乐亦大，他无足云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234391_comment'></div>未间盖练器业，前报宠休。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1234391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　友人范茂直卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　作《谢主文陈用中》二首，有年老怀才不遇之感。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年10月</a>　有蔡姓道人云刚中“廷试当在第三，春试当为第一”。作品：《送相人蔡道人序》<div id='poem_1234598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送相人蔡道人序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234598")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234598'>绍兴辛亥冬十月，有相士姓蔡者，自号碧云道人，访予于金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234598_comment'></div>予时已冒礼部，蔡道人云：「廷试当在第三，春试当为第一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234598_comment'></div>留小诗一绝，其末云：「学馆色如蓝，不作鳌头亦第三」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234598_comment'></div>余不敢领，又坐贫，无以酬之，因其求诗，谩书以付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234598_comment'></div>俟道人术信，则持此书以见余。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1234598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　赐进士及第，授左文林郎，温州军事判官。作品：《赐第后告祖庙文》<div id='poem_1234695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐第后告祖庙文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234695")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234695'>某爰自丱角，考妣付之师友，使读书，事科举，非谓某可教也，盖上世之业不可坠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234695_comment'></div>去年礼部上某名于天子，天子策问而官之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234695_comment'></div>忝窃科名，遂叨仕版，非某之能也，盖上世之德覃于后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234695_comment'></div>持牒奉告，君命惟宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234695_comment'></div>拜陈于庭，惟我曾大父下逮考妣之灵鉴之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1234695_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月</a>　友蒋持志亡。作品：《蒋持志墓志铭》<div id='poem_1234684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒋持志墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234684")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234684'>婺之浦江蒋氏，有讳承汉者，生子用亨，用亨生浃，皆隐居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234684_comment'></div>浃生真，真字持志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234684_comment'></div>持志蚤年警悟，善记诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234684_comment'></div>某初游学校，见其文采详华，人物古澹，场屋间朋辈推高，已加爱重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234684_comment'></div>其后某升贡去乡里，日怪其淹延未鸣，乃云持志收裹笔砚，掉臂而归者久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234684_comment'></div>闻其有言曰：「舍法向敝，文体卑弱，士气不振，乃失己为名之时，循此以求进，非吾所能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234684_comment'></div>遂阖户不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234684_comment'></div>今方聚书辟馆，料理田园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234684_comment'></div>赀产饶裕而优游深肆，足以涵养其业，益知君有过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234684_comment'></div>建炎中，盗起君舍旁，弄兵大剽，乃尽弃其财，挺身亡去，论者谓持志积以遗盗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234684_comment'></div>迨王师纵火加兵，民居之在中者亦不能辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234684_comment'></div>他日君归寻其区，则墙屋不毁，文籍窗几如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234684_comment'></div>人然后信其德于乡邻，虽盗不忍加不仁，王师过之，亦知其居为君子之居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234684_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234684_comment'></div>学者为进取所累，揣合俯仰，苟且求售，其能脱然疏远科名、探本求道者固鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234684_comment'></div>至于事生产作业者，则又多不识取予积散之术，无以善富，故黩货嗜利，无厌以自及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234684_comment'></div>如君之为学为家，皆无愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234684_comment'></div>君天性简约，颜面严冷，童稚皆知畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234684_comment'></div>门巷幽洁，所与游者，必一时佳士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234684_comment'></div>平生未尝以私事溷官府，而井里有争者，则多取决于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234684_comment'></div>绍兴二年五月丙午，以病渴而卒，享年五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234684_comment'></div>娶职方外郎陈确之孙、进士汲之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234684_comment'></div>二男子：曰次乂，游上庠，志趣激昂，行能可喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234684_comment'></div>曰次夔，禀资厚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234684_comment'></div>是皆可以光大君后者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234684_comment'></div>三女子：长适乡贡进士陈某，次适进士汪某，次许嫁进士陈某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234684_comment'></div>孙男三人：曰槐、松、柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234684_comment'></div>卜以其年月日，葬于某地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234684_comment'></div>次乂泣血致书，以乡人冯光之状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234684_comment'></div>某于君雅故，义不得辞，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1234684'>学而不为名所拘，富而不为财所累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234684_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234684_comment'></div>持志可以无愧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1234684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　刚中归家途中遇大雨，友董彦明授以饮食车马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　与蒋惠民学于金华。作品：《送蒋惠民序》<div id='poem_1234600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送蒋惠民序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234600")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234600'>蒋惠民，宣和庚子从余学于浦江，绍兴癸丑从余学于金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234600_comment'></div>庚子距癸丑，盖十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234600_comment'></div>中间惠民娶妻长子，兵火艰难，无所不有，而好学之志益坚，相从之意益厚，其蕴蓄于中者，益滋润可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234600_comment'></div>呜呼，可谓贤也已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234600_comment'></div>然庚子之学，始正月至十一月，不三百日而余去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234600_comment'></div>癸丑之学，始正月至八月，不二百日而子归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234600_comment'></div>其相与群居，皆不逮久，余复运斤手老，不知能果尽子鼻端之翼否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234600_comment'></div>念此后余当试吏，而子亦行有良图，宦游东西，后面何日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234600_comment'></div>于其告行，诵曾子之言而送之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234600_comment'></div>其言曰：「尊其所闻，则高明矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234600_comment'></div>行其所知，则光大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234600_comment'></div>高明光大，不在于他，在乎加之意而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234600_comment'></div>子其勉哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1234600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1134')">1133-1134年</a>　任温州军事判官。作品：《癸丑年暖阁初成》<div id='poem_174749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸丑年暖阁初成</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174749")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174749'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174749'>枯叶寒梢夜夜声，围炉小阁喜初成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174749'>护风帘密香烟润，弄日窗低书卷明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174749'>况有酒浆初暖热，从他岁律自峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174749'>块然危坐得佳处，万事人间一唾轻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174749_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174749'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174749_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月</a>　刚中友余彦诚以疾卒于寝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月23日</a>　任温州军事判官。作品：《甲寅九月末雨至十月二十三日得晴闻是日六飞进狩诸将告捷》<div id='poem_174835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲寅九月末雨至十月二十三日得晴闻是日六飞进狩诸将告捷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174835")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174835'>密雨重阴一月馀，似闻征马又长驱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174835'>怪来林外升晴日，已奏江边报捷书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174835_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7933d7e36d434b1c976dabaed71af8bb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7933d7e36d434b1c976dabaed71af8bb");'><span id='7933d7e36d434b1c976dabaed71af8bb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>，48岁</div><div id='7933d7e36d434b1c976dabaed71af8bb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　友余彦诚归葬。作品：《余彦诚墓志铭》<div id='poem_1234686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>余彦诚墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234686")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234686'>建隆初，睦之遂安余氏有讳钟者，徙居婺之义乌，再世而生荣，荣生喜，喜生明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234686_comment'></div>彦诚盖明之季子，讳信，彦诚其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234686_comment'></div>某异时游义乌，过流庆陂，见其旁有民田数千亩，比岁沃稔，问之邑人，则曰：「彦诚用家钱百万修废堰，潴源水，遇旱岁，无高下彼我均浸之，邻里沾足」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234686_comment'></div>予尝叹曰：「余氏其昌乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234686_comment'></div>设心如此，必有过人者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234686_comment'></div>既而闻彦诚果好义轻财，折节下士，虽高赀巨产雄视一乡，率皆因低昂积散，知予为取，而坐制其利，乡人无不称其长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234686_comment'></div>故纷争斗怒者，得其一言则释然以平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234686_comment'></div>宣和庚子，青溪盗起，浙东西诸郡往往失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234686_comment'></div>彦诚纠率里豪，捍蔽乡曲有奇功，大帅上其名，补承信郎，调青州准备差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234686_comment'></div>居官以廉谨闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234686_comment'></div>是时燕云初复，人皆张皇自得，彦诚被檄往来幽蓟间，常忽忽不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234686_comment'></div>语其僚曰：「虏情叵测，而漫不为备，正犹狎虎豹而去其闲，咆吼之患，近在朝夕，盍早图之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234686_comment'></div>度无有能用其言者，遂解官求罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234686_comment'></div>既归，则又语所亲曰：「时危矣，与其无益而死，曷若奉亲教子以终馀日」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234686_comment'></div>当路交辟，不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234686_comment'></div>绍兴四年五月甲寅，以疾卒于寝，享年六十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234686_comment'></div>彦诚为人倜傥尚气，雅好宾客，至终日忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234686_comment'></div>宗族贫窭、姻戚孤嫠、知交流落者，斥帑廪济之，无不得所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234686_comment'></div>事继母尤孝，家道肃睦，内外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234686_comment'></div>晚嗜佛书，诵之寒暑不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234686_comment'></div>家旁双林寺，寇东南兵火后，数年为墟，彦诚倡始施财，不踰时而还万楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234686_comment'></div>其馀津梁断坏病涉之地，靡不修举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234686_comment'></div>盖其心志开朗，凡所为数皆落落可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234686_comment'></div>某初与彦诚昧平生，因其辟馆舍，遣子弟迎予犹子瑱者为师，礼意频年不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234686_comment'></div>一日过其门，瑱率舍中后生数辈罗列藏书，质问义理，率秀嶷不凡，彦诚从容其间，一话言皆有激勉教诲之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234686_comment'></div>由是深得彦诚之用心，遂为相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234686_comment'></div>乙卯二月，某将之官永嘉，公之孤汝评、叔龄相与踵门而请曰：「先子卜葬有日，圹中之铭，窃愿有托」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234686_comment'></div>某非但义不得辞，亦喜为彦诚撰述平生之事，悲而许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234686_comment'></div>彦诚娶同里王氏，生两男子：汝评，承信郎，避公讳，就校尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234686_comment'></div>叔龄，右迪功郎，和厚而通敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234686_comment'></div>一女子，适士人许师颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234686_comment'></div>孙男五人：文焕、文粹、文炳、文质、文昌，皆力学进业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234686_comment'></div>自汝评而下，其所成就，异日当有可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234686_comment'></div>王氏先十有二年而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234686_comment'></div>彦诚以乙卯某月某甲子，葬于双林乡蜀墅源，从王氏之藏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234686_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1234686'>富其家又仁其里，禄其身亦昌其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1234686_comment'></div>诸孙诜诜，业以书史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1234686_comment'></div>徜徉暮年，其寿而死，余之喜为彦诚铭者以此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1234686_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='34af56c8b9e041acbb4e0f9a699cd6af_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("34af56c8b9e041acbb4e0f9a699cd6af");'><span id='34af56c8b9e041acbb4e0f9a699cd6af_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>，61岁</div><div id='34af56c8b9e041acbb4e0f9a699cd6af' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年8月11日</a>　于横溪之阳种田数亩。作品：《记旱》<div id='poem_1234661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234661?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记旱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年8月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234661")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234661'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234661'>绍兴戊辰，岁无秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234661_comment'></div>郑子硗田不数亩，在横溪之阳，旱穗犹可捋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234661_comment'></div>八月十一日，与租客分取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234661_comment'></div>是日大热，张小盖坐大田中，无林木可依，左右烘炙，去暍死无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234661_comment'></div>忽自谓曰：「居无苦乐，随吾所安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234661_comment'></div>物无小大，生于所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234661_comment'></div>以乐视苦，以大视小，安知今日焦热之非清凉也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234661_comment'></div>既作是念，目前种种闲旷，阡陌委曲，如深檐广庑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234661_comment'></div>禽鸟往来，如幽人佳客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234661_comment'></div>一块之土，高于泰山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234661_comment'></div>一根之蔓，茂如乔松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234661_comment'></div>俯视蝼蚁蚯蚓之窍，亦邃然幽隐，有岩谷之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234661_comment'></div>微风入凋丛瘁叶之间，佳声飒然，小盖翻飞，而长空炽焰，已化为婵娟万顷之寒浸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234661_comment'></div>御风之兴，泠然不浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234661_comment'></div>郑子然后知动静哀乐，穷通得丧，大率如是，当作一理观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234661_comment'></div>蜗角有绵蛮之国，非庄生过论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234661_comment'></div>作《记旱<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山文集》卷五。）</span>》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234661_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1234661'>绍兴戊辰：「绍兴」原作「建兴」，按宋无建兴年号，当为「绍兴」之误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234661_comment'></div>绍兴戊辰即绍兴十八年，与刚中生存年代符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234661_comment'></div>据改。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1234661_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
浦江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='97d36c37191e4ae6aedd31caa676509c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97d36c37191e4ae6aedd31caa676509c");'><span id='97d36c37191e4ae6aedd31caa676509c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1122')">1120-1122年</a>，33-35岁</div><div id='97d36c37191e4ae6aedd31caa676509c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　郑母归土，挈家入浦江，作学堂，教人子弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　蒋惠民从郑刚中学于浦江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1122')">1121-1122年</a>　郑刚中在浦江办学。作品：《辛丑正月十三饮南厅》《罪回禄并引》《寓灵峰寺感怀》《灵峰闻秋雨》《双莲膏露辨并序》<div id='poem_174879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛丑正月十三饮南厅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174879")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174879'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174879'>小槽沥沥流香乳，玉壶注入金鹦鹉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174879'>甘脆铺陈荐肴俎，环炉数客不停举。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174879'>酒酣耳热灯前舞，呼呜不作儿女语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174879'>未到山颓且撑拄，窗外濛濛正春雨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174879'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174879_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_175002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_175002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/175002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>罪回禄<span class='inlineComment2'>（并引）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_175002")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_175002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_175002'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_175002'>回禄为火神，威权尤贵重。<div id='poem_sentence_0_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_175002'>年来何失职，权为盗所弄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_175002'>此盗假尔威，蜂蚁聚徒众。<div id='poem_sentence_2_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_175002'>煌煌万炬光，灼燎随所纵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_175002'>烟氛障白日，烘炙盛骚动。<div id='poem_sentence_4_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_175002'>老幼哭无家，祸虐人所共。<div id='poem_sentence_5_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_175002'>使人不见此，聪明欲何用。<div id='poem_sentence_6_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_175002'>神而审其然，可得亡制控。<div id='poem_sentence_7_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_175002'>忍使盗意满，生民负焦痛。<div id='poem_sentence_8_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_175002'>尔过不可文，反躬当自讼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_175002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_175002'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_175002_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寓灵峰寺感怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174990")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174990'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174990'>遥风入林筱，淅沥生夜愁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174990'>明月过窗牖，照此虚室幽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174990'>念从出怀绷，志在承箕裘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174990'>唯知业书卷，何尝识戈矛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174990'>去年妖寇兴，尽破东南州。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174990'>烟来走官吏，火过成墟丘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174990'>豺虎恣搏噬，鼯鼪啸朋俦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174990'>砧俎血忠义，罝网罗善柔。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174990'>皇皇势窘急，有罅即愿投。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174990'>挈妻负幼子，敢谓生可偷。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174990'>潜遁得幽僻，如鱼初脱钩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174990'>妥尾定惊胆，馀魂渐能收。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174990'>今者王师来，元凶已拘囚。<div id='poem_sentence_12_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_174990'>巢窟有馀类，尚此稽讨搜。<div id='poem_sentence_13_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_174990'>参商隔弟妹，阻塞无书邮。<div id='poem_sentence_14_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_174990'>家在北山口，烟林裹沧洲。<div id='poem_sentence_15_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_174990'>更此乱离后，当无一椽留。<div id='poem_sentence_16_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_174990'>何但一堂庐，最苦悲松楸。<div id='poem_sentence_17_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_174990'>使我思归梦，枕边清泪流。<div id='poem_sentence_18_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_174990'>嗟嗟庙堂客，为国须早谋。<div id='poem_sentence_19_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_174990'>积薪从下燃，谁云无后忧。<div id='poem_sentence_20_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_174990'>愿令弄兵者，依旧操锄耰。<div id='poem_sentence_21_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_174990'>勿俾太平世，虮虱生鞮鍪。<div id='poem_sentence_22_174990_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_174990'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_174990_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>灵峰闻秋雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174877")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174877'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174877'>夜静荷池叶翻翻，声如珠玑落冰盘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174877'>小窗客梦忽惊破，知是秋雨来池间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174877'>清晓阴云压前山，凉风飘萧起林端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174877'>病身便觉衣袂薄，蒲葵已作无情看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174877'>田家喧呼各相劝，年丰可望糠籺宽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174877'>更愿朝廷念东南，吾侪自勉加盘餐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174877'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_174877_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>双莲膏露辨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234650")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234650'>侍郎梅公宣和壬寅夏四月出为蕲州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234650_comment'></div>秋八月，郡池有莲，并蒂而华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234650_comment'></div>越冬日至，膏露降于松，浃三十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234650_comment'></div>公不敢自当其瑞，既归报于上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234650_comment'></div>蕲之士夫，复不能掩公之德也，则为赋为序，为诗为歌，翕然颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234650_comment'></div>表甥郑某自念学术荒替，而又揄扬咏道之谱尽为诸公所先，不复更可摹画，姑取他人漏落馀意，穿凿而足其说，再拜献于堂下，名曰《双莲露辨》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234650_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1234650'>郑子一日问蕲之老人曰：「知若太守之瑞乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234650_comment'></div>曰：「知之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234650_comment'></div>「能言其所以乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234650_comment'></div>曰：「能之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234650_comment'></div>郑子使之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234650_comment'></div>老人曰：「吾太守令严而政简，信顺和洽，欺诬屏息，薰然流入草木烟露间，故今效祥如此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234650_comment'></div>郑子曰：「噫嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234650_comment'></div>水芝骈蒂，天酒成膏，虽学语小儿，亦知为和气所感，尚奚从老人问之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234650_comment'></div>盖以土物之生，蕃鲜而萼者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234650_comment'></div>花之双也，何众卉无与，而独见于莲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234650_comment'></div>曲直而枝者多矣，露之降也，何凡木不受，而独在于松？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234650_comment'></div>若不如此，而谩谓和气所召，无乃昧化工之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234650_comment'></div>吾今为若辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234650_comment'></div>莲之为物，泥不能污，水不能著，脱卑垢而自致于清明之上，盖花之至净者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234650_comment'></div>今太守志明行洁，教化清净，皎皎如秋月孤高，尘埃不可翳障，非莲无以瑞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234650_comment'></div>松之为物，宽容庇下，蟠固错落，犯岁寒而冬夏不能易其操，盖木之至坚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234650_comment'></div>今太守心正气刚，节义森薄，凛凛与霜雪争严，炎凉不可变易，非松无以瑞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234650_comment'></div>不然，荻笋包泥，蒲柳柔脆，顾可使之为瑞乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234650_comment'></div>今人知莲与松之为瑞，而不知其所以为瑞，能为双花膏露为说，而不能为莲与松言之，此吾所以不得不辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234650_comment'></div>虽然，物瑞君子之所罕道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234650_comment'></div>吾与若辈虽铺陈附会，以累太守，安知调和雨旸，惠养一方，使蕲民饱暖嬉笑，知有为生之乐者，太守自有上瑞也耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234650_comment'></div>老人唯而退，郑子于是乎书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1234650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　南游离白沙。作品：《壬寅年南游离白沙》<div id='poem_174814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬寅年南游离白沙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174814")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174814'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174814'>木杪日未升，四野落寒雾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174814'>昏濛失冈峦，咫尺见行路。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174814'>我独何区区，犯此寒色去。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174814'>重伤寄蹇身，百事已迟暮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174814'>既不早冲跃，要津先自据。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174814'>又无二顷田，林泉闭门户。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174814'>方此念友朋，升斗活车鲋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174814_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
