-----title
道县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b3cb426389b34ad8b703310f6da066e4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b3cb426389b34ad8b703310f6da066e4");'><span id='b3cb426389b34ad8b703310f6da066e4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>，35岁</div><div id='b3cb426389b34ad8b703310f6da066e4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年10月26日</a>　郑刚中南游。作品：《宣和壬寅十月余游江南二十五日道出月岩方崇宁甲申先子休官长沙挈家人宿岩下此后二十年间哭父母失姊妹祸患百端今日虽使余富贵过此尚当悲感不自已况复羁孤无聊为万里旅人耶欲作一诗梗切未能就止以二十八字叙其事翌日得四韵（二首）》<div id='poem_174915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣和壬寅十月余游江南二十五日道出月岩方崇宁甲申先子休官长沙挈家人宿岩下此后二十年间哭父母失姊妹祸患百端今日虽使余富贵过此尚当悲感不自已况复羁孤无聊为万里旅人耶欲作一诗梗切未能就止以二十八字叙其事翌日得四韵<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年10月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174915")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174915'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174915'>石漏摇空一片天，月岩之号古相传。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174915'>孤轮高洁谁为比，老树婆娑亦宛然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174915'>山碍不容千里见，崖侵常蚀二分偏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174915'>故知伪物谁叨冒，终竟天教不十全。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174915'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174915_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174916?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年10月26日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174916'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174916'>先亲膝下共游人，孤影飘零只我身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174916'>今日再来如隔世，泫然衰泪落江滨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174916'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174916_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
抚州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c2b4a4fa66294daea4398c029e3e8e12_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c2b4a4fa66294daea4398c029e3e8e12");'><span id='c2b4a4fa66294daea4398c029e3e8e12_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>，35岁</div><div id='c2b4a4fa66294daea4398c029e3e8e12' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年11月26日</a>　郑刚中南游。作品：《宣和壬寅仲冬二十六日留别临川陈泰颖》<div id='poem_174917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣和壬寅仲冬二十六日留别临川陈泰颖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年11月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174917")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174917'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174917'>江南浙东千里摇，雁聚沙汀无定迹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174917'>偶然握手如平生，祗恐前身已相识。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174917'>不然安得一羁旅，披露烦君出金石。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174917'>我今漂泊又西去，草草分襟实堪惜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174917'>孤舟漾水如轻叶，何处烟村倚滩碛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174917'>明朝横枕清浪头，梦破霜风正相忆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174917'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_174917_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f4db7bedbb114e98bd82197ca3ad9b9c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f4db7bedbb114e98bd82197ca3ad9b9c");'><span id='f4db7bedbb114e98bd82197ca3ad9b9c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>，36岁</div><div id='f4db7bedbb114e98bd82197ca3ad9b9c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　仲冬倚舟钱塘，见康才老。别叶彦法。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='04be424644ba4ba4be924a616e0803c6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("04be424644ba4ba4be924a616e0803c6");'><span id='04be424644ba4ba4be924a616e0803c6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1139')">1136-1139年</a>，49-52岁</div><div id='04be424644ba4ba4be924a616e0803c6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　秋，召赴行在所，未至，除详定一司敕令所删定官。既至，赐对，改左宣议郎，除枢密院编修官。作品：《论责实疏》<div id='poem_1234325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论责实疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234325")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234325'>臣闻人君之道，内在于尽诚，外在于责实，诚实备至而天下不治者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234325_comment'></div>陛下比年宽刑罚，省科徭，戒贪赃，严警备，恤饥穷，每一诏下，丁宁恳恻，其思治望道之心，计亦切矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234325_comment'></div>然而百姓不尽知，德泽不遍及者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234325_comment'></div>责实有所未至尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234325_comment'></div>天下君子少，小人多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234325_comment'></div>臣子效职者少，欺陛下者多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234325_comment'></div>朝廷施行一事，付之监司，监司付郡守，郡守付县令，各了一司文移之具，不问其有无实惠及民，是则虽尧禹在上，功效何由而著乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234325_comment'></div>故民间往年闻宽厚之诏，犹咨嗟怨恨，曰：「吾君爱民如此，而官吏弗之行也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234325_comment'></div>今则不然，美意一颁，天下知其为虚设尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234325_comment'></div>盖欺罔诞谩之弊，至今不革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234325_comment'></div>广设文具，应办目前，髣髴近似，以报其上，故视其已具之文，虽陛下不能无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234325_comment'></div>吾法既美矣，吾官吏亦奉行如此矣，一何治道之难成！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234325_comment'></div>曾不知有名无实，受陛下之惠者，百不一二有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234325_comment'></div>陛下以诚意鼓众动化，立中兴之治，而官吏乃至变移之，岂不痛乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234325_comment'></div>尝观汉宣帝之所行，成帝亦行之，而治功为不及者，盖总核名实，孝宣帝之所长故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234325_comment'></div>元康二年，孝宣即位十载矣，方下诏与士大夫厉精更始矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234325_comment'></div>今陛下临御亦十年，而天下有虚文之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234325_comment'></div>臣愿为士大夫下厉精之诏，许自今宣布实德，视斯民利害，如在其家，如在其身，不得虚名文具欺罔朝廷，使陛下之诚意被覆赤子之身，而不在于官府文书之上，则枢机周密，可以不愧汉宣帝之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234325_comment'></div>苟为不然，因循苟且，日复一日，必累陛下责实之政也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1234325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　作《忠义堂记》<div id='poem_1234662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234662?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忠义堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234662")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234662'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234662'>永嘉州治之北，有堂曰忠义，前太守程公之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234662_comment'></div>绍兴丙辰，端明殿学士、礼部尚书会稽李公来镇是邦，既见吏民，问疾苦，颁条教，约与为清净之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234662_comment'></div>一日过其上，顾谓僚属曰：「是堂规模闳伟，而创立命名之因，无所稽考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234662_comment'></div>吾闻鲁公唐人之英，言忠义者莫先焉，后五世流落为温人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234662_comment'></div>鲁公末年，亲书告牒，其家传宝之，郡尝为刊于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234662_comment'></div>尔者天子官其家永嘉者二人，家乐清者一人，所以彰遗烈而播馀芳者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234662_comment'></div>虽鲁公之名，所在咸仰，要之此邦乃其遗迹流风之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234662_comment'></div>吾今求其像绘置堂上，徙其石刻列之两旁，使后人知堂名之有属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234662_comment'></div>公等以为宜乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234662_comment'></div>幕吏东阳郑某避席改容而言曰：「真卿，小邾子颜公子友之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234662_comment'></div>自颜含为晋侍中，相传七叶，皆以忠孝名世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234662_comment'></div>至有唐真卿、杲卿，以堂兄弟门户并立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234662_comment'></div>杲卿常山之名既凛凛如霜雪，希烈之变，真卿复振显于后，天其以忠义萃一门乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234662_comment'></div>尝考鲁公上世，凡能尽忠于国者，无不以孝行称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234662_comment'></div>由是知善为臣子者，于忠孝之道初未尝析。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234662_comment'></div>后世道德不纯，风俗凋落，臣子分两途，始以忠义为难事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234662_comment'></div>至若鲁公处死之节，论者伟之，而识者犹以为不足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234662_comment'></div>观其平日议论慷慨，落落难合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234662_comment'></div>唐旻诬之，李峘非之，李辅国、元载、卢杞辈怨恨切骨，而公益自信，知爱君忧国而不知祸之及己，此盖能以事亲者事其君故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234662_comment'></div>忠义，天下之大闲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234662_comment'></div>偷生假息固可以延乱臣贼子之命，而英声伟烈常出于奸鈇逆鼎之旁，二者唯人所自择而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234662_comment'></div>公为政之初，暴扬兹美，非但可以慰颜氏之精爽，亦足以销杞、载、辅国千古粪壤奸人之气，其谁曰不宜」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234662_comment'></div>公曰：「众以为宜，则子为我记于石」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1234662_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　祈雨中元水府。作品：《祭中元水府文》《丁巳年七月二十一日祈雨中元水府八月六日展谢祠下皆被旨也然祷后越七日始雨神所为耶其不然也审自神出不无愆期之尤有如不然神之饕上赐也多矣为诗以问之》<div id='poem_1234718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭中元水府文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年7月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234718")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234718'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234718'>旱久伤稼，皇帝忧动颜色，谓神之能以云雨出灵者，惟中元最闻，命小臣郑某祝于祠下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234718_comment'></div>二十一日，某既致命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234718_comment'></div>念其还也，非得霔雨嘉泽以报天子，则某所以为朝廷来者，无乃虚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234718_comment'></div>九重彻膳以俟，而乃不得报以归，罪宜如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234718_comment'></div>王以水府之尊，爵号显著，人所钦事，天子遣使祝辞，而邈然无所报称，则自馀以灵感望神者，将疑而怠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234718_comment'></div>使者微甚，宜勿为神所听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234718_comment'></div>王者号令百神，使之受职，其庸可忽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234718_comment'></div>又况时方孔艰，丰凶所系，神亦有焉，当能一二鉴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234718_comment'></div>谨再拜告王以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234718_comment'></div>尚享。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1234718_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁巳年七月二十一日祷雨中元水府八月六日展谢祠下皆被旨也然祷后越七日始雨神所为耶其不然也审自神出不无愆期之尤有如不然神之饕上赐也多矣为诗以问之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年8月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174795")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174795'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174795'>奉祝出阊阖，祷雨祠中元。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174795'>陈祠信已荐，拱俟心亦虔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174795'>山云屡触石，散去如飞烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174795'>惭衷迫秋阳，汗流颈徒延。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174795'>趑趄念亡状，归马不敢鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174795'>云台欲旬浃，蹇兆方解悬。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174795'>皇慈喜嘉霔，报贶礼弗偏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174795'>谓乃百神功，共相成丰年。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174795'>遣昨致祠吏，奔趋各如前。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174795'>我载谒水府，意惑口莫言。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174795'>黄屋四海心，责已汤未贤。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174795'>抑畏动黎庶，精诚格高圆。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174795'>正恐三日雨，帝敕下九天。<div id='poem_sentence_12_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_174795'>神令享丰报，然乎其不然。<div id='poem_sentence_13_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_174795'>贪功认有者，鄙贱人所怜。<div id='poem_sentence_14_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_174795'>神聪冠四渎，宜弗蹈尔愆。<div id='poem_sentence_15_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_174795'>益思赞元化，后效图所先。<div id='poem_sentence_16_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_174795'>小臣此将命，芒刺终未捐。<div id='poem_sentence_17_174795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_174795'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_174795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月</a>　帝书羊祜传赐予郑刚中。作品：《拟跋御书羊祜传》<div id='poem_1234618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟跋御书羊祜传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234618")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234618'>绍兴七年九月，宗祀明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234618_comment'></div>前二日，皇帝书晋《羊祜传》五千四百二十九字，以赐臣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234618_comment'></div>臣既再拜受赐，命良刻摹入琬琰，奉墨本藏之什袭，为私门世世之宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234618_comment'></div>复再拜而言曰：孙皓失德，虐据吴氏，地险力悍，未易取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234618_comment'></div>惟祜专务抚循，使晋朝之德如阳春暖日，行于积阴之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234618_comment'></div>和气既至，冰冻皆不约而解，所以吴不得存，长江不得阻，而晋已混有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234618_comment'></div>皇帝陛下以威武镇艰难之运，以仁厚申祖宗之德，虽城中赤子，暂谓南北，而兼爱之心，同一视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234618_comment'></div>祜书之作，岂但游神翰墨，灿奎璧而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234618_comment'></div>垂休黎元，意盖有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234618_comment'></div>顾臣老矣，不足以对扬盛美，俟布宣德惠有如祜者出，为陛下奏平吴之策，于时臣当自山林间捧持宸翰，稽首阙廷，躬上万岁之觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234618_comment'></div>臣无任区区。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1234618_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　春，权尚书左司员外郎，除尚书考功员外郎，为贡院参详官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年7月</a>　权尚书左司员外郎，除尚书考功员外郎，为贡院参详官。作品：《论有司奉职持法奏》<div id='poem_1234326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论有司奉职持法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴八年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234326")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234326'>说者谓有阳而无阴，不可以成岁功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234326_comment'></div>有德而无刑，不可以成政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234326_comment'></div>臣常惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234326_comment'></div>今试使一人持刻薄之说，劝人主为苛察之政，则有识者必指为法家者流，是欲置天下于浇疵怨谤之地，不可听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234326_comment'></div>又使一人持宽大之说，劝人主为姑息之政，则有识者必指为败法之人，是欲置天下于委靡不振之域，亦不可听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234326_comment'></div>臣反覆计虑而后得其说，盖宽仁者人主之道，持法者臣下之职，二者不可易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234326_comment'></div>人主与天地同德，惟高明博厚，然后公公私私，有生能言之类各足其欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234326_comment'></div>至于百官有司，则法度之所在，犹四时之气，推行造化，可生则生，可长则长，可肃则肃，可杀则杀，予夺之间，不可有毫釐之谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234326_comment'></div>惟使生育之恩归于上，法度之章谨于下，四海之内戴君父之德而畏有司之严，然后朝廷尊而政事修矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234326_comment'></div>恭惟祖宗以恺悌之风荡五代之毒螫，陛下以泽润之德救百六之涂炭，累圣相承，前后一轨，大君之道，咸不约而得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234326_comment'></div>考其忠厚之极，则无如仁宗皇帝之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234326_comment'></div>慈惠之气，盎然如春风者几五十载，覆载之功，不为不大，然所谓法度者，未尝弛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234326_comment'></div>内之朝廷，外之郡县，有人犯一非义，则郡守必劾，监司必按，台谏必言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234326_comment'></div>以至一官资之予夺，一刑名之轻重，一钱谷之出入，有司各守其法以争之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234326_comment'></div>不得于法，虽力彊势重，不敢有徼幸之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234326_comment'></div>小大同心，共以身任之而不顾，天下惟见人主简易优游，坐收宽仁之名，而天下亦无敢为非者，此祖宗与三代治古之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234326_comment'></div>至陛下临御以来，宽仁爱物之心于古有光，而臣下持法之心颇与古异，大率有司皆不肯以身任怨责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234326_comment'></div>县有罪，郡守不敢劾，留以俟监司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234326_comment'></div>守有过，监司不敢按，留以俟台谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234326_comment'></div>某事于法不可行也，郡犹问于监司，监司问六部，六部问朝廷，朝廷作圣旨罢之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234326_comment'></div>某事于法不可得也，郡犹请于监司，监司请六部，六部请朝廷，朝廷作圣旨夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234326_comment'></div>积日累月，罢之夺之，皆自一人出，而百官有司无一拂戾人情者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234326_comment'></div>苛察之怨日渐归于上，姑息之恩各欲归诸己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234326_comment'></div>此岂善风俗持久之道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234326_comment'></div>诸葛孔明曰：「宠之以位，位极则贱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234326_comment'></div>顺之以恩，恩竭则慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234326_comment'></div>是故吾绳之以法，法行则知恩」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234326_comment'></div>善乎其能言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234326_comment'></div>盖法者，百王相授之具，上下守之，而皆出于无心，惟使宽宥旷荡之泽，时出于人主，则天下皆若履秋霜之严而知有春阳之暖，岂不伟欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234326_comment'></div>皋陶为士，将杀人，尧曰宥之三，皋陶曰杀之三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234326_comment'></div>夫皋陶岂不知将顺之美，以谓宥罪者人君之恩，至有司则奉法而已，不知其它也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234326_comment'></div>此后世所以乐尧宥刑之宽，而畏皋陶执法之坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234326_comment'></div>臣愿陛下戒敕臣吏，各使持职奉法，凡予夺之际，自有成书，无大疑惑者，不得互相推避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234326_comment'></div>其失职废法，全身避怨者，咸按督之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234326_comment'></div>常使纪纲持循，赏罚明信，不废法度，而陛下宽厚之仁，泊然与覆载同功，俾天下独知斯谋斯猷，惟我后之德，则生灵幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1234326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　以考功郎兼右司，因职事暂寓天竺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　秋，除监察御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　刚中请辞监察御史。作品：《辞监察御史疏》<div id='poem_1234295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞监察御史疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234295")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234295'>臣田野寒生，造化遗物，科名甚晚，吏琐何卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234295_comment'></div>朝廷召从远方，置在枢属；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234295_comment'></div>阅岁未再，试以郎曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234295_comment'></div>臣方夙夜省循，惧无以报称万分，而陛下又亲擢而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234295_comment'></div>夫六察，中台之要选也，岂臣阘茸无状者之所宜冒处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234295_comment'></div>欲责报效，宜付贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234295_comment'></div>伏望睿慈收还误恩，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1234295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　刚中外孙生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年11月</a>　刚中外姑归葬。作品：《外姑墓志铭》<div id='poem_1234687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>外姑墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234687")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234687'>浦江进士杜諲妻谢氏，生女晬而諲死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234687_comment'></div>后四年，谢携其女再适故赠朝请郎何至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234687_comment'></div>至育之十年，择同邑士者石子文归之，今孤子石知彰之母夫人是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234687_comment'></div>夫人生三男：长曰知彰，次知柔、知言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234687_comment'></div>女三人：长适具位郑某，次适士人郑玠，次适承节郎何邦献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234687_comment'></div>某顷闻石大人用干蛊弃笔砚，夫人申申恨之，叹曰：「吾父业儒蚤死，今吾夫学又废，奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234687_comment'></div>会朝请公之子粲登上舍第，夫人歆慕感激，谓知彰辈眉目皆秀，必可泽以仁义，故力为求师友，又以巽女见妇，冀诸子得游从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234687_comment'></div>盖于时石氏蕃大，非豪门不姻，人见以所爱女归一寒士，家贫姑严，营糠豆而事礼法，皆不以为乐，独夫人甘心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234687_comment'></div>其后某虽忝窃科名，可以少塞相贵重之意，然知彰病复不能卒业，知柔出为伯父采之后，为举子者独知言一人，而夫人死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234687_comment'></div>养所不能泊也，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234687_comment'></div>夫人庄靓寡言，动有仪则，凡妇道治内之美无一不备，盖以女子而知儒学之贵，其资性可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234687_comment'></div>绍兴戊午三月，来访其女于临安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234687_comment'></div>六月甲子，感微恙而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234687_comment'></div>七月甲子，知言辂柩以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234687_comment'></div>十一月甲子，葬于邑之南溪园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234687_comment'></div>石大人初葬不吉，先以丙辰十月甲子徙南溪，故夫人祔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234687_comment'></div>夫人享年六十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234687_comment'></div>方诸子尝药不逮之辰，夫人顾谓某曰：「三魁石氏，名称高甚，尝惧吾诸子不克髣髴，今安得一言而死，使兄弟相勉，念先业而思奋，庶几吾不赍志而没地也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234687_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234687_comment'></div>览《寒泉》劳苦之咏，诵《蓼莪》劬瘁之诗，斯言可忘哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234687_comment'></div>某既为之铭，左朝散郎、尚书吏部员外郎黄圭书之，左朝请大夫、司封员外郎曹琏题其额，俾知彰刻而藏之云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234687_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1234687'>坦冈原，奥水泉，兹为南溪之园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234687_comment'></div>兆斯迁，祔旁穿，石氏考妣藏之庆延绵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1234687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　冬，除殿中御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　刚中请辞殿中侍御史。作品：《辞殿中侍御史疏》《自劾奏疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（参郑文《送蒋惠民序》）</span><div id='poem_1234296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞殿中侍御史疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234296")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234296'>臣禀资甚愚，立志良苦，比由考功郎官，蒙陛下亲擢，缪参六察之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234296_comment'></div>未淹三月之久，督稽违而无效，念忝窃以知惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234296_comment'></div>窜斥之虞，朝夕以俟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234296_comment'></div>荐加器使，敢复叨居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234296_comment'></div>今世态方艰，事功未济，耳目之任，殿中执法者实共司之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234296_comment'></div>顾臣何人，可冒兹选！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234296_comment'></div>伏望收还成命，更付良士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234296_comment'></div>非但公朝王论之有托，亦微臣愚分之少安。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1234296_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234307?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自劾奏疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234307")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234307'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234307'>臣闻臣之事君，贵在不欺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234307_comment'></div>子之事父，可以情恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234307_comment'></div>虽值雷霆之怒，敢陈蝼蚁之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234307_comment'></div>臣比缘北使在馆，计议不决，于十二月二十三日，与御史中丞句龙如渊、右谏议大夫李谊连名入奏，乞于二十四日同赴都堂，见宰执商议，圣旨许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234307_comment'></div>缘当日所议未尽，复连奏，乞二十五日再赴都堂，圣旨许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234307_comment'></div>议定，理须躬禀圣训，复连奏，乞二十六日合班上殿，圣旨又许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234307_comment'></div>忽于二十五日晚，宣押句龙如渊、李谊赴内殿奏禀，而臣不与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234307_comment'></div>臣忧惧惶惑，不知所处，即欲阖门待罪，而国事未定，人情不安，小己之私，岂敢辄布！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234307_comment'></div>今也使事已定，群听交孚，臣可以恳祈陛下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234307_comment'></div>臣闻台谏之官，天子以为耳目，盖所亲信而不疑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234307_comment'></div>官有小大，而受责则同，陛下呼台谏议事，而臣独不与，必臣于和议之计有不可与闻者，其为耳目也疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234307_comment'></div>祸福之几，系于使事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234307_comment'></div>计谋不臧，缪以千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234307_comment'></div>陛下呼台谏议事，而臣独不与，必臣于和议之计而不能宣力者，其为耳目也废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234307_comment'></div>居陛下耳目之任既疏且废，虽圣庭包容，未加诛窜，而臣负此二罪，岂得自安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234307_comment'></div>陛下方收拾俊彦，图济艰难，必得有气节之人聚之朝廷，然后他日可责以事功之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234307_comment'></div>使臣侥倖误恩，但知苟禄，则陛下亦何所用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234307_comment'></div>人不劾臣，臣当自劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234307_comment'></div>伏望圣慈罢臣殿中侍御史职事，特赐黜责，庶协公议<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山文集》卷一。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234307_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1234307'>值：原无，据库本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1234307_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月</a>　上书论边境守臣。作品：《论边郡守臣疏》<div id='poem_1234327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论边郡守臣疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴八年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234327")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234327'>臣窃谓张官置吏，皆以为民，而治外之官尤重于郡守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234327_comment'></div>承流宣化，莫先于太守，而今日之势尤急于边郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234327_comment'></div>甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234327_comment'></div>边郡之欲得人，臣请为陛下详言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234327_comment'></div>在内诸郡，簿书狱讼，户口农桑，财赋盗贼，是数者有一不治，皆足以为害，然患小势缓，而所系犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234327_comment'></div>至于边郡，则维持控扼，与国势常相关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234327_comment'></div>抚绥不至，则生齿凋而力孤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234327_comment'></div>备御不严，则罅隙开而衅入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234327_comment'></div>巡徼不谨，则奸伪容而谋泄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234327_comment'></div>关市不修，则物货艰而钱陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234327_comment'></div>朝廷非可谩委以付人，得一人亦非可轻以更易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234327_comment'></div>三国魏据中原，自广陵、寿春、沔口之属，皆其东边也，而吴亦以所抵为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234327_comment'></div>南安、祈山、陈仓之属，皆其西边也，而蜀亦以所抵为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234327_comment'></div>大率曩之为魏者，今多在北敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234327_comment'></div>曩之为吴蜀者，今皆在朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234327_comment'></div>如楚、泗、通、泰，以至滁、濠、江、鄂，接连襄、邓、关陕之地，为今边郡者，大略不过二三十郡，委以与人，诚不可忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234327_comment'></div>臣愿陛下诏大巨详阅吏琐，将诸处见任及已除未到之人精加审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234327_comment'></div>访求材术之士，略其细行，但平时绩效著闻，实可任用者，精选二十馀辈，布之边郡，使其讲究利源，招徕士卒，种殖牧养，蕃息疲瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234327_comment'></div>分委既定，时遣朝廷官吏按行省察，取其无状者复更易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234327_comment'></div>俟其处处得人，则须以持久，增秩赐金之事可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234327_comment'></div>朝廷亦何惜数阙，必欲以资任终更？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234327_comment'></div>亦何轻数郡，但欲作寻常委付耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234327_comment'></div>昔韩延寿善为郡，所在置正长，闾里阡陌有非常，吏辄闻知，奸人莫敢入界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234327_comment'></div>又晁错为文帝陈守边备塞之说甚详，大要欲使著业安居，家室田作，为久远之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234327_comment'></div>所用之吏，存恤老弱，善遇壮士，和辑其心，而无侵刻之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234327_comment'></div>由是观之，陛下用以守边者宜加审择，既得其人，宜加久任无可疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234327_comment'></div>或谓臣曰：「朝廷和议既成之后，故地可还，今日所谓邻边者，却为内郡，势若可缓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234327_comment'></div>此大无理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234327_comment'></div>人君立国，惟在因时，本无定势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234327_comment'></div>借使故地果因通和而还，则要当以江淮为根本，所谓故地者却是新民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234327_comment'></div>根本殖立于内，护之当益工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234327_comment'></div>新民屏蔽于外，倚之当以渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234327_comment'></div>更须数年经理，力彊势重，始可望其通一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234327_comment'></div>所谓江淮者，在今日尤当爱重也，故臣切切以边郡守臣为言，望陛下与二三大臣留意选择，特赐施行，不胜幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1234327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月14日</a>　胡铨因上书请斩秦桧，此日被贬送吏部与广南监当。台鉴勾龙如渊、李谊、郑刚中等上疏共解救。作品：《申救胡铨疏》<div id='poem_1234303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申救胡铨疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年12月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234303")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234303'>臣窃闻枢密院编修官胡铨上书论使事，其言狂悖，力诋大臣，圣恩宽容，闻止除名，送昭州编置，可谓父母之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234303_comment'></div>然臣区区尚欲一言者，非谓铨无罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234303_comment'></div>臣独以陛下南渡以来，未尝拘顾忌讳，逐一言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234303_comment'></div>岂不以时方艰难，事功未济，与其罪狂夫而容有后悔，曷若并包并受，以来天下之言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234303_comment'></div>故内怀一槩者，虽伸吭感激，怨咨天地，陛下率听而纳之，如是者有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234303_comment'></div>今也岂不能容一胡铨，以增盛德之光乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234303_comment'></div>重念铨一介书生，坐无思虑，但闻众论汹汹，不知使事曲折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234303_comment'></div>原其用意，亦为爱君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234303_comment'></div>铨本贯吉州，奉老母于此，铨窜远去，母将畴依？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234303_comment'></div>陛下方孝友格天，欲成和议，若置铨于圣度之内，使其子母相保，不至狼狈，诚莫大之恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234303_comment'></div>臣不胜祷祈之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234303_comment'></div>冒犯天威，罪当万死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1234303_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月18日</a>　郑刚中上言钱观复性资阴狠，台章数论气短，故罢钱观复。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年12月25日</a>　郑刚中论尚书驾部员外郎王居修缘大臣姻故，遽叨郎选。上罢之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　请除宗正少卿。作品：《除宗正少卿书》<div id='poem_1234313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除宗正少卿疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234313")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234313'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234313'>臣自幼读书，惟务行己，晚而筮仕，但知爱君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234313_comment'></div>至于智虑暗愚，材力绵薄，则叨冒器使之初，尽恳祈于陛下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234313_comment'></div>然臣待罪殿中，今才两月，凡所论奏，悉荷包容，有可施行，即蒙采听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234313_comment'></div>此臣所以昕夕自誓，愿效万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234313_comment'></div>而适当多事之日，略无展力之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234313_comment'></div>陛下使居耳目之任，而下情不以上闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234313_comment'></div>使居风宪之地，而奸佞不能力去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234313_comment'></div>则是陛下所以待臣者，不啻天地父母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234313_comment'></div>而臣之所以图报者，可谓孤神明而负寸心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234313_comment'></div>按其亡状，付之司败，臣亦流涕而知恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234313_comment'></div>若犹怜之，俾从补外之禄，臣尤刻骨而怀感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234313_comment'></div>属籍亚卿，地清职峻，厚颜以处，臣亦何安！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234313_comment'></div>伏望圣慈收还成命，与一在外合入宫庙差遣，庶安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1234313_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　春，除宗正少卿，移秘书少监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　夏，为枢密行府参谋，出谕京陕，左宣教郎。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1176f87850674670a4d98810aaa3b4dc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1176f87850674670a4d98810aaa3b4dc");'><span id='1176f87850674670a4d98810aaa3b4dc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1141')">1139-1141年</a>，52-54岁</div><div id='1176f87850674670a4d98810aaa3b4dc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　郑刚中出谕京陕，行府所至，选将帅，隶军马，访疾苦，经用度，以至表扬忠义，撰《请除罪籍奏》。<div id='poem_1234310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请除罪籍奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234310")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234310'>臣检会今年正月五日赦书内一项，新复州县见停废文武官将校公吏，未经甄叙人，并许赴所在自陈，保明以闻，当议时与甄叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234310_comment'></div>臣窃详刘豫僭窃，逆天悖道，谓之有功者，实助豫为虐之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234310_comment'></div>谓之有罪者，未必真坐累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234310_comment'></div>今豫所录者，朝廷包含混贷，捐其旧恶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234310_comment'></div>豫所斥者，朝廷从而弃之，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234310_comment'></div>方使无辜抱恨之人，伸吭自诉，有司锱铢原减，论如常程，则是朝廷尚为伪齐行法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234310_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞应新复州县官吏、军民被罪，有文字照验者并不理遗阙减降，未经叙复者，即依本等叙复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234310_comment'></div>内有元因刘豫补受，复为刘豫废夺者，永不在甄叙之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234310_comment'></div>庶几罪功两平，众论惟允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1234310_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　郑刚中出谕京陕，《褒进三老疏》疑为其途中所作。<div id='poem_1234315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>褒进三老疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234315")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234315'>臣初入陕西，即访问高行之士，有奉议郎、前原州通判米璞，朝请郎、前知陇州刘化源，奉议郎、前签书博州判官厅公事刘长孺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234315_comment'></div>士民众口一辞，谓璞当废齐乱常、群伪争进之日，杜门谢病，终不受污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234315_comment'></div>关陕之人见璞则知有朝廷，今虽童稚能道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234315_comment'></div>化源守陇，孤城既陷，虏守视之，不得死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234315_comment'></div>驱入河北，鬻蔬果，隐民閒十年，卒不屈辱以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234315_comment'></div>长孺当逆豫萌凶之日，尝致书备陈祖宗德泽，劝其转祸为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234315_comment'></div>豫怒，毁除告牒，囚之百日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234315_comment'></div>后复起之以官，长孺坚卧自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234315_comment'></div>三人皆本贯耀州，业儒登科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234315_comment'></div>乱离以来，糠豆不赡，而高风善行，蔼然有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234315_comment'></div>臣于本州津致前来，亲加劳问，而璞苦风痹，右足几废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234315_comment'></div>化源等已老，步履亦艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234315_comment'></div>虽作圣旨行下，发赴行在，缘以老病，各不能就道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234315_comment'></div>伏望圣慈怜其陷没之久，察其志节之高，特与除宫观差遣，仍进官一二等，偿其闲废之日，使璞等优游祠禄，为乡曲门户之荣，实圣朝激励风俗之道也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1234315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　冬，除权尚书礼部侍郎，转左通直郎，寻兼详定一司敕令，又兼权尚书刑部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　尚书礼部侍郎兼权尚书刑部侍郎。作品：《辞免权尚书礼部侍郎劄子》《辞免试尚书礼部侍郎劄子》<div id='poem_1234316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免权尚书礼部侍郎劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234316")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234316'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234316'>臣困顿馀生，奇孤弱植，脱身下吏，厕迹周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234316_comment'></div>蒙陛下奖擢之恩，已非一日，展力从事者亦屡试矣，迄无片善，可效万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234316_comment'></div>未从司败之诛，缪窃道山之禄，兹复叨冒，人其谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234316_comment'></div>又况宗伯之司，国之所重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234316_comment'></div>贰卿之职，其选甚高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234316_comment'></div>法从清联，朝廷所以命士，非若庶工之冗，容可以一介充也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234316_comment'></div>侧听已行之命，实怀非据之忧，仰翼鸿慈，俯从愚悃，收还恩宠，以副公言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1234316_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免试尚书礼部侍郎劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234317")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234317'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234317'>臣学识荒疏，人材猥下，摄官宗伯，误蒙器使之恩，而黾勉周皇，寸长不效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234317_comment'></div>已知踰分，更俾即真，不恳祈君父而求避焉，则公朝铨择之鉴，臣实累之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234317_comment'></div>伏望圣慈收还成命，别选通才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234317_comment'></div>庶几可以佐官长之讨论，措礼文于隆盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1234317_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年11月</a>　上书言治理三京。作品：《论保养三京之道奏》<div id='poem_1234328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论保养三京之道奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234328")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234328'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234328'>臣闻人君之有天下，犹人之有四体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234328_comment'></div>人之四体，惟血气浃洽，脉络流通，然后疾病不生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234328_comment'></div>一者有痞塞，则肤理为之不荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234328_comment'></div>人君之天下，惟德意交孚，政事遍举，然后危乱不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234328_comment'></div>一者废隔，则纲纪为之不贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234328_comment'></div>国家多故以来，江淮之北，阴邪之气结为痈疽，聚为痼癖者，不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234328_comment'></div>赖陛下感动天地，强敌革心，和气一通，而大河以南妖沴平息，甚盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234328_comment'></div>臣今年四月被旨为枢密院行府参谋官，渡江踰淮，道京洛，抵关陕，尝为陛下详观今日天下之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234328_comment'></div>关陕新复而且远，然其就绪也必易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234328_comment'></div>三京去东南为近，然其就绪也尚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234328_comment'></div>关陕就绪矣，三京之力又从而相接，则关陕之安，久而可保；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234328_comment'></div>苟三京之力衰敝不振于中，则关陕孤绝，后当有可虑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234328_comment'></div>臣请备言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234328_comment'></div>陕西诸路虽号新复，然得禁军可四万，皆壮勇善战之人，是官不至于无兵也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234328_comment'></div>弓箭手旧额一十四万，今犹得六万，是民尚可以为兵也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234328_comment'></div>年谷既狼戾，官中见管之粟与和籴相当，共可以足一岁之食，是土地不全旷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234328_comment'></div>今又益之以秦凤、熙河出蜀之兵，宣抚使节制其间，有一旦之警，利兵据险，六经略趋走而闻号令，未易窥也，臣故曰就绪为易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234328_comment'></div>惟洛阳百战之馀，凋残尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234328_comment'></div>其西则陕府为邻，陕自李彦仙死守，虏悉力取之，民无噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234328_comment'></div>其东则汴京、应天府一带，久为刘豫凶焰所焚，焦痛未苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234328_comment'></div>三京户口，今计虽仅四十万，比平时不能十分之三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234328_comment'></div>近又缘屯田司收其已租之田，追其元买农具，公私相碍，宿麦不入土，民力殊困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234328_comment'></div>论其地势，则平川通道，不见藩篱，无一兵可以受甲，无一家可以输上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234328_comment'></div>孤城乍聚之众，不相统属，衅隙之所易生，臣故曰就绪为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234328_comment'></div>夫关陕先就绪而三京不能振起，则朝廷之德意政事痞塞于数千里之间，有如盗贼蒙死徼幸，乘执事之不备，则潼关以西，不过自能保守，当无气力相援，纪纲废隔，岂不再贻关陕之忧哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234328_comment'></div>臣愿陛下与二三大臣讲究所以保养三京之道，选任名德重望之士置之要郡，审择材猷敏博之吏使为监司，增广戍兵而谨备不虞，精究屯田而俾民安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234328_comment'></div>使朝廷和气自东南达乎西北，中间血气浃洽，脉络流通，起居食息，日就安彊，则事功之兴起未易量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234328_comment'></div>苟惟不然，肤理不荣，复有受病之处，不治将深矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1234328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　尚书礼部侍郎兼权尚书刑部侍郎。作品：《己未十二月二日致斋惠照》《跋左达功所示李泰发诗卷》<span class='inlineComment2'>（郑刚中《跋左达功所示李泰发诗卷》曰：“宣和丁酉，某以桑梓拜天台左先生于金华……后二十二年，达功相访临安……”姑系于此年。）</span><div id='poem_164157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_164157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/164157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己未十二月二日致斋惠照</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年12月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_164157")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_164157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_164157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_164157'>坛殿夜漫漫，临祠愧礼官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_164157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_164157'>降神欣乐奏，望瘗肃更阑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_164157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_164157'>雨意垂檐黑，风声过竹寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_164157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_164157'>晓庭人寂寞，乌鸟拾馀残。<div id='poem_sentence_3_164157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_164157'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_164157_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋左达功所示李泰发诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234619")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234619'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234619'>宣和丁酉，某以桑梓拜天台左先生于金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234619_comment'></div>于时达功才十岁许，侍立先生之旁，照人如玉笋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234619_comment'></div>后二十二年，达功相访临安，而衫犹未青也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234619_comment'></div>高材淹泊，乃至是耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234619_comment'></div>既而诵参政李公四诗，见其称道许与如此，知达功富贵不晚矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1234619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年2月</a>　上书论驭将帅之道。作品：《论驭将帅当恩威并用奏》<div id='poem_1234329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论驭将帅当恩威并用奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234329")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234329'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234329'>臣闻人主之恩，天也，含容包覆，混贷惟一，故人无不悦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234329_comment'></div>人主之威，雷霆也，摧压震曜，超忽变化，故人无不畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234329_comment'></div>有如偏废，则是犹太虚廓廓，而不示以风雷之象，生物之功，无造化矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234329_comment'></div>矧其驾驭桀黠、延接雄隽之际，所以笼络控制，收其心而折之气者，宜又如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234329_comment'></div>臣伏闻陕西二三大帅被旨入觐，旦夕且至，陛下高官显服焕宠其身者既无不周，祥风庆泽荡涤其意者又无不尽，彼方蒙戴惩省感激悼惧之不暇，陛下引见之日，所以劳徕抚存，推诚意而收其心者，虽不可后，至于释罪宥过，责以后效而折其气者，正宜摧压震曜，示以风雷之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234329_comment'></div>不然，位极则贱，恩极则慢，恐有不知朝廷之尊者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234329_comment'></div>英布之归汉也，高祖踞床见之，布大怒悔来，欲自杀，出就舍，又大喜过望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234329_comment'></div>夫淮南亦乱世之奇杰，不背楚，则汉取天下，未有万全之策，功亦大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234329_comment'></div>然高祖所以见之之礼尊严如是，曾不以半言摩拊，诚以诈力权变之士，初拔身以归，安知无恃功矜德广己造大之心，故高祖先求所以折服之者，而徐以厚意慰藉之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234329_comment'></div>非特如此，光武之受赤眉也，陈兵临洛水，而问盆子曰：「汝知当死否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234329_comment'></div>其众请命，则又曰：「得无悔降乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234329_comment'></div>吾不强服汝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234329_comment'></div>众皆屈服，然后陈其三善而释之，人赐田宅，各使以妻子居洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234329_comment'></div>又闻太祖皇帝一日饮王审琦等酒，而与之语，明日相率乞罢兵权、奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234329_comment'></div>是必有以感动其心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234329_comment'></div>今日入觐之臣，朝廷所以待遇之者，圣心自有恩威之度，臣敢以区区之说为陛下言之者，盖亦狂瞽之愚，有不能自已也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1234329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年4月</a>　左中奉大夫符授归葬。作品：《左中奉大夫致仕符公神道碑》<div id='poem_1234682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左中奉大夫致仕符公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234682")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234682'>鲁顷公之后，有仕秦为符玺令者，以符为氏，传汉唐五代，家世可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234682_comment'></div>建昌南丰之符，盖今世之名族也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234682_comment'></div>左中奉大夫致仕符公，是为南丰之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234682_comment'></div>公讳授，字天启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234682_comment'></div>曾大父俸，大父怀德，皆隐德弗耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234682_comment'></div>父明远，累赠金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234682_comment'></div>金紫公已读书自奋，然庆喜之泽，犹涵閟未发，众知其必有子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234682_comment'></div>公生果不群，器度明爽，洽闻彊记，辞华如绮，场屋老生敛笔避之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234682_comment'></div>中元丰二年进士第，调兴国军司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234682_comment'></div>丁母南康郡夫人瞿氏忧，服除，调卲州卲阳县主簿，就移筠州上高县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234682_comment'></div>终更入远为彭州录事参军，改京秩，差歙州婺源县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234682_comment'></div>丁金紫公忧，服除，知越州剡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234682_comment'></div>用年劳升朝，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234682_comment'></div>秩满，差通判龙州，未行，户部辟主管在京左厢店宅务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234682_comment'></div>又通判海州、唐州，旋提点西京崇福宫，再提举江南太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234682_comment'></div>渊圣即位，覃恩转朝议大夫，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234682_comment'></div>今上嗣历，覃恩转左中奉大夫，遇郊恩封南丰县开国男，食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234682_comment'></div>公解褐入仕，历五朝六十年而归禄告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234682_comment'></div>绍兴乙卯，某为温州判官，公之子行中通守是邦，决除秕政，利敏难事，而又论议踔厉，志行峻洁，无一分巧宦计，僚士窃议是必名教积习所致者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234682_comment'></div>或曰：「此南丰符中奉子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234682_comment'></div>中奉一生静退，雅不与躁进者争急流，至其耿耿胸次者，则贲、育不能折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234682_comment'></div>枢密吴公居厚尝荐之于朝，且使见宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234682_comment'></div>公曰：「筦库何伤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234682_comment'></div>自媒求进，其伤实多」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234682_comment'></div>终户部官，足不至时政之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234682_comment'></div>逮题舆海邦，专务简约，凡椎剥刻深之政，应奉媚悦之事，断然不为，而公亦低徊向老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234682_comment'></div>某由是详公之为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234682_comment'></div>岁戊午，某备员行在所，闻公之夫人汤氏前一年卒，公已上章挂冠，亟遣书行中，慰其母夫人之忧，且使为偏侍节哀，善事中奉，致期颐安荣之养，则孝子之心尚有馀乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234682_comment'></div>越庚申，行中以黄州童使君之状，为公丐神道碑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234682_comment'></div>读其状，盖己未十二月辛酉以疾终于正寝，庚申四月己酉，已葬太平乡石榴原，合汤夫人之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234682_comment'></div>悲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234682_comment'></div>公为人端庄清净，有信义，无声色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234682_comment'></div>蚤岁儒雅缘饰，翰林杨绘颇推重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234682_comment'></div>有《南丰居士诗》十二卷，平澹峻激，杂见于波澜动静之间，自成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234682_comment'></div>当官号令简严，而遇繁必办，所至吏不敢逞，逞则锄尽之乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234682_comment'></div>民间爱慕，咸父母怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1234682_comment'></div>其在上高，尝与高安两令易，二邑之民争于境上，今犹以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1234682_comment'></div>晚年志意萧散，耳目聪明，对灯火读细字书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1234682_comment'></div>享年八十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1234682_comment'></div>男五人：长建中，右承议郎、知信州贵溪县，次用中：皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1234682_comment'></div>大中，右迪功郎、监潭州南岳庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1234682_comment'></div>行中，左朝奉郎、主营台州崇道观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1234682_comment'></div>幼未名而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1234682_comment'></div>女二人：长适右迪功郎、临江军清江县尉辛爽邦，次适右奉议郎、通判韶州上官闵，亦前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1234682_comment'></div>孙男十二人：勤、愿、逊、悊、𢘍，皆登仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1234682_comment'></div>忞、宪、思、憙、恕、怘、愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1234682_comment'></div>孙女七人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1234682_comment'></div>汤夫人，处士详之女，有贤行，与公齐年，归符公甲子凡一周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1234682_comment'></div>大中、行中才皆适用，久奉亲不肯出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1234682_comment'></div>每岁时，老人雍容堂上，二子帅诸妇孙子捧觞上寿，庭间炜然，人皆指为偕老之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1234682_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1234682_comment'></div>爵禄犹滋味也，人所同嗜，公独安义命，守澹泊，不为滋味所毒，而平生所享，比他人往往反为甚丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1234682_comment'></div>彼有贪饕冒昧足陷无厌之域者，一失所嗜，并与所当得者失之，闻中奉之风有愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1234682_comment'></div>某既知公为详，而黄州之状复缄以来，其可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1234682_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1234682'>符氏德善，著于南丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1234682_comment'></div>有閟其祥，发之自公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1234682_comment'></div>公之文章，以取科第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1234682_comment'></div>陶冶锻鍊，亦传永世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1234682_comment'></div>公之政事，克振厥职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1234682_comment'></div>岂弟详明，为后之则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1234682_comment'></div>弗争而进，弗取而得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1234682_comment'></div>富贵寿考，众如公何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1234682_comment'></div>石榴之原，兆久窾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1234682_comment'></div>黄土苍苔，公则掩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1234682_comment'></div>镌彼金石，载此铭诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1234682_comment'></div>维其邦人，实咏歌之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1234682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　秋，以年劳转左奉议郎，遇明堂恩，封荥阳县开国男，食邑三百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　冬，除试尚书礼部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　作《庚申岁焚黄祭文》<div id='poem_1234724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234724?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚申岁焚黄祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234724")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234724_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234724'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234724'>某绍兴七年，以文林郎为枢密院编修官，品视升朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234724_comment'></div>明堂敕恩，封赠如法，皇考承事赠宣教郎，皇妣盛氏赠孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234724_comment'></div>维吾考妣，不以某为愚而命之学，择师友以成其业，躬桑苧以济其须，德不我负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234724_comment'></div>而嗣承不肖，蚤弗冲跃，方挂冠垂老，倚门寡瘁，计日待养之时，乃困穷场屋，左颠右仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234724_comment'></div>岁三十二，布其衣，木惊风矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234724_comment'></div>呜呼，尚忍言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234724_comment'></div>逮今进官晚成，叨尘禁地，回首慈容，皆在泉壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234724_comment'></div>虽能躬持告牒，奉上君恩，祗为痛尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234724_comment'></div>而又赠典得于丁巳，副黄焚于庚申，中间扈从往来，参佐南北，实未皇暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234724_comment'></div>今复予告严程，迫于王命，遽成展省，礼仪未修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234724_comment'></div>谨迟后日之归，申焕再郊之宠，亦尚休哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234724_comment'></div>尚享。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1234724_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年4月</a>　上书言收韩世忠、张俊、岳飞兵权。作品：《与宰相书》（窃见降制）<div id='poem_1234353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与宰相书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二　绍兴十一年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234353")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234353'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234353'>窃见降制，除三宣抚为枢密副使，以其兵归枢密院，合朝廷中外之势，通诸帅彼我之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234353_comment'></div>凡前日天下以为忧、以为难者，一旦变为平易安强之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234353_comment'></div>庙堂之上，声色如故，三大帅惟恐奉上兵籍之不先，一何盛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234353_comment'></div>虽然，利害得失常对倚而不废，遇事更变则激发而复起，就其利不忘其害，见其得愈忧其失，而后可以大有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234353_comment'></div>伏愿相公周思熟计，益善其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234353_comment'></div>其试以所见，条列于左方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234353_comment'></div>沿边州县，倚兵为安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234353_comment'></div>比自淮甸蹂践之后，人情往往忧危，大帅又舍之而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234353_comment'></div>给罢之初，传闻或失实，远地何知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234353_comment'></div>一家狼顾，馀皆相和而惊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234353_comment'></div>俾知本末，不可无告喻之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234353_comment'></div>三宣抚之兵，纪律不同，平日分而用之，各安其所主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234353_comment'></div>他日合而用之，固有以更屯易帅为便者，亦有顾恩念旧而不能忘者，安慰人心，当有混一之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234353_comment'></div>三宣抚所分之地，平日有警，便各任责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234353_comment'></div>今既只是统制将官在外，有如尘高敌厚，使谁纠合而前？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234353_comment'></div>必待飞檄告急，然后朝廷遣发，晚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234353_comment'></div>豫为期约，当有应卒之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234353_comment'></div>宣抚司诸将首领，尽是收拾散亡与杀降剧贼，其间悍狠虐下，顽钝嗜财，荡淫纵欲者，色色皆有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234353_comment'></div>平时畏大帅不得逞，一旦释去，其陵损士卒，交相货利，藏匿子女之弊，岂得无之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234353_comment'></div>弹压整齐，当有画一之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234353_comment'></div>君子可以义劝，小人可以利诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234353_comment'></div>前日诸帅恐其下有见利而逸者，故或质其文书，属其妻子，以系累其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234353_comment'></div>今一旦去其统帅，敌人朝暮伺之，垂钓设饵，宁无贪啖之人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234353_comment'></div>然则察视防闲，当有杜绝之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234353_comment'></div>宣抚司教阅之法，最号严肃，垂赏示劝，人人精进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234353_comment'></div>今既分立头项，其淬砺思奋、立功自拔者，必多有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234353_comment'></div>至荒废燕安、苟且自便者，安得无也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234353_comment'></div>训练作成，当有劝沮之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234353_comment'></div>诸军钱粮，专系总领司应办，宣司按月勘请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234353_comment'></div>所有器甲，尽系朝廷颁降，宣司量事分给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234353_comment'></div>今宣司既罢，合渐就法制，使无冒请之弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234353_comment'></div>立为准程，使无损阙之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234353_comment'></div>《传》曰：「平乱责武臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234353_comment'></div>相公以道佐人主，提纲振领而收其成功，军旅之事，宜尽以责右府，经画曲折，一一使之思虑，相公酌其可否，裁其议论，付之使行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234353_comment'></div>他日进退攻守，彼皆不得以为言矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1234353_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年4月</a>　郑刚中为秦桧陈善后七策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　夏，除宝文阁直学士、枢密都承旨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　除宝文阁直学士、枢密都承旨。作品：《辞免宝文阁直学士枢密都承旨劄子》《谢除宝文阁直学士枢密都承旨表》<div id='poem_1234318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免宝文阁直学士枢密都承旨劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234318")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234318'>五月八日，准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，除臣宝文阁直学士、枢密都承旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234318_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234318_comment'></div>臣窃以侍郎分曹治事，其选高矣，而密承上旨者，其职为尤重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234318_comment'></div>阶官辨秩为等，品已贵矣，而升华内阁者，其资为甚崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234318_comment'></div>兼以付之，则朝廷委用之意，盖自可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234318_comment'></div>而臣禀资驽下，赋性愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234318_comment'></div>怙恃已无，虽有一意事君之愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234318_comment'></div>而筋力向暮，实怀十驾难及之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234318_comment'></div>冒昧以居，愆尤将至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234318_comment'></div>伏望圣慈收还成命，别付时髦，外穆师言，下安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234318_comment'></div>臣无任皇恐激切恳祈之至，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1234318_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除宝文阁直学士枢密都承旨表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234351")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234351'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234351'>久玷清曹，宜招大戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234351_comment'></div>遽移要地，仍冠华资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234351_comment'></div>识睿奖之优隆，抚微躬而震越<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234351_comment'></div>窃以国有二柄，古列鸿枢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234351_comment'></div>事分五房，均承上制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234351_comment'></div>爰自熙宁而后，始参用于士人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234351_comment'></div>故兹承旨之员，或旁兼于史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234351_comment'></div>诚以斗极执化元之本，机廷为宥密之亲，拱侍天墀，躬聆帝训，宜求洵直，克用禀承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234351_comment'></div>而况西清宝栋之崇，实仁庙宸章所秘，服是邃严之职，并为儒雅之流，兼以授人，谁宜蒙者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234351_comment'></div>伏念臣性资愚下，学艺浅荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234351_comment'></div>触事多艰，渐觉桑榆之向慕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234351_comment'></div>戴恩甚重，常如山岳之在巅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234351_comment'></div>念从召用而来，误被眷知之宠，超腾省户，擢副台端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234351_comment'></div>观秘书者，顷尝一年，奉典礼者，今亦踰岁，率无善状，可穆师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234351_comment'></div>荐拜鸿私，惟知感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234351_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下照临如日，覆冒法天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234351_comment'></div>独运乾刚，总六师而并用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234351_comment'></div>大修机政，开二府以兼收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234351_comment'></div>图回不世之功，尽革累年之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234351_comment'></div>兹所选任，宜先俊良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234351_comment'></div>夫何庸琐之才，亦在访咨之数！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234351_comment'></div>臣敢不周旋体国，恪检持身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234351_comment'></div>虽惧疏愚，无补枢机之密；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234351_comment'></div>誓磨顽顿，少酬造化之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234351_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1234351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年10月</a>　上书乞准许荐举。作品：《乞许荐举奏》<div id='poem_1234330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞许荐举奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234330")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234330'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234330'>被旨，所过州县许按察官吏，除治行显著、罪犯明白之人合行闻奏外，欲乞许令荐举改官亲民任使七员，堪充从事郎、县令任使十员，庶几有以奖进人材。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1234330_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1234330'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》职官四一之一○（第四册第三一七一页）。又见同书选举二九之三○（第五册第四七○九页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1234330_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='43bb5e587da043d29c7313868eb8c673_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("43bb5e587da043d29c7313868eb8c673");'><span id='43bb5e587da043d29c7313868eb8c673_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，47岁</div><div id='43bb5e587da043d29c7313868eb8c673' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　游岳麓山。作品：《先君守官醴陵日予尝随先生读书岳麓山法华台上时年一十五今兹再来四十有七年矣置榻设几之处历历可寻感而赋》<div id='poem_174848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先君守官醴陵日予尝随先生读书岳麓山法华台上时年一十五今兹再来四十有七年矣置榻设几之处历历可寻感而赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174848")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174848'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174848'>愚翁髫髦昔垂耳，曾向华台借窗几。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174848'>小冠短褐随先生，风雨孤灯读经史。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174848'>气粗胆大眼无人，拔擢犀象角连齿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174848'>那知物外有沆瀣，但欲书中觅青紫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174848'>尝持杯酒望高城，吊彼洛阳年少子。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174848'>棘闱裹饭三十年，百炼自知俱绕指。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174848'>后来脚蹈官职场，恩重如山报无几。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174848'>今兹疏发蓬霜颠，踪迹旧游真愧耻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174848'>一松一石如雅故，应笑愚翁今乃尔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174848'>愚翁明日便南去，岁月曷其重致此。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174848'>凭栏之恨在无言，珍重湘西山与水。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174848_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174848'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_174848_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5519cbd460414f32950e49f6bea2450f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5519cbd460414f32950e49f6bea2450f");'><span id='5519cbd460414f32950e49f6bea2450f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>，48岁</div><div id='5519cbd460414f32950e49f6bea2450f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，赴温州判官任。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>郑刚中官永嘉。作品：《送符正民罢倅永嘉》《与康才老》<div id='poem_174940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送符正民罢倅永嘉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174940")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174940'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174940'>去年敛板趋庭侧，门前杨柳如金色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174940'>今年公去柳何如，已作凉阴舞寒碧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174940'>岁月忽匆无足恨，离合人生那免得。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174940'>身如汀雁偶相逢，自是不须论定迹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174940'>我今胡为抱不满，攀辕益为邦人惜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174940'>永嘉雄望城海滨，吏久不良民弊积。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174940'>年来开府皆钜公，旁助刬除知有力。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174940'>岁当乙卯夏不雨，旱雾吹风千里赤。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174940'>爱人节费惜锱铢，廪廥单穷犹足食。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174940'>北方兴师日千金，州县皇皇虑供亿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174940'>溥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>哉时发仁人言，未至取鱼忧竭泽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174940'>青衫幕吏有何能，造物见怜相抆拭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174940'>自知愚拙生霾雾，临事昏蒙无远识。<div id='poem_sentence_12_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_174940'>天机遇触狂态作，掐鼻炙眉成痼癖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_174940'>唯公道眼借馀青，颇许披心露真率。<div id='poem_sentence_14_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_174940'>人生感恩未易言，正恐不能同木石。<div id='poem_sentence_15_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_174940'>仙才秀骨公所有，化作文章可华国。<div id='poem_sentence_16_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_174940'>持身况若玉壶冰，透里无尘只清白。<div id='poem_sentence_17_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_174940'>暂分半刺聊尔耳，此岂能令公议塞。<div id='poem_sentence_18_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_174940'>行当摆脱州县冗，下跨秋风开六翮。<div id='poem_sentence_19_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_174940'>夔龙有室俱可入，愿吐诗书资硕画。<div id='poem_sentence_20_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_174940'>自馀强饭无足云，转首潮平江树隔。<div id='poem_sentence_21_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_174940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_174940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_174940'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_174940_0'>⑴ 原作博，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_174940_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1234428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与康才老</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234428")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234428'>某咨目拜上才老奉议：癸卯仲冬，倚舟钱塘，仅得一见之后，非但顿挫无聊，而世故攲危，变态百出，游魂假息，常如鼎中鱼，非不念异时倾盖不可忘，而东西阻塞，兼与广口绝往来之便，无从探伺动息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234428_comment'></div>近抵浦江，如闻使车暂此憩止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234428_comment'></div>审惟别后吉德契天，行己无愧，神明俱赞，尊候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234428_comment'></div>某奇蹇馀生，偶叨绅笏，得官永嘉，坐待远阙，诸况如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234428_comment'></div>法慧之款，回首十年，其寺今虽再立，比前时不能十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234428_comment'></div>去岁期集，偶置局其间，凡吾人笑歌灯火之地，尽为瓦砾之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234428_comment'></div>遗址依然，每一过之，尚如小阁夜半望友人未至之时也，其如倾想何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234428_comment'></div>某寓邑中，更须旬日，相望一舍，无缘参谒，临书增情而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234428_comment'></div>或尚从容广口，此后当图求见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234428_comment'></div>区区有怀，非面莫既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234428_comment'></div>自馀唯祝保练，前迓殊宠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1234428_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
