-----title
徽县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ca50e4090e0b4ca7a5760554808c0e1f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ca50e4090e0b4ca7a5760554808c0e1f");'><span id='ca50e4090e0b4ca7a5760554808c0e1f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1142')">1141-1142年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='ca50e4090e0b4ca7a5760554808c0e1f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　冬，除宝文阁直学士，为川陕宣谕使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年12月23日</a>　郑充陕西路分画地界官，应干措置委川陕宣抚司南北誓书文字，仔细分画，不得差错生事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年12月25日</a>　朝廷又命刚中分画陕西，以刘豫、吴玠原管地界为准。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　刚中外孙生，名之曰蓬孙。作品：《蓬孙小名序》<div id='poem_1234631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蓬孙小名序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234631")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234631'>章郎生子之月，余新除监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234631_comment'></div>书至其家，德文小名其子曰台孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234631_comment'></div>邢郎生子之月，余以秘书少监出陕西，得诏遣书见报，且请小名其子，余名之曰蓬孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234631_comment'></div>乌台、少蓬，皆借外祖官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234631_comment'></div>他时两孙长大登科，书小录能念老人否？</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1234631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年1月</a>　奏请与金画地界。作品：《与北人画地界事奏》<div id='poem_1234323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234323' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234323?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与北人画地界事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234323")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234323'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234323'>臣所与北官商议，其初欲尽取阶、成、岷、凤、秦、商六州，论难往复，渐次听从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234323_comment'></div>其确然欲得者，秦州、商州、和尚原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234323_comment'></div>三处乃川陕咽喉要害之地，皆不可轻许，而和尚原最为不可，此原内蔽四川，而尤切于凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234323_comment'></div>金人在原口，我得凤州无益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234323_comment'></div>失凤州，内有仙人关，川固未能遽入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234323_comment'></div>但骑兵长驱，历兴州而至梁、洋，三郡路平如掌，并无限隔，我以轻兵戍之，势决不保；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234323_comment'></div>悉重兵屯之，粮道不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234323_comment'></div>当是时，川之一臂枯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234323_comment'></div>宣司之兵，今多屯于梁、洋，若凤州危，则阶、成、岷悉在外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234323_comment'></div>数郡岁供和籴近二百万，一旦动摇，则梁、洋之兵必不能聚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234323_comment'></div>欲收以入川，四川不能尽给也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234323_comment'></div>商州在南山诸谷之间，为金、洋、均、房之门户，外有七盘关，下瞰长安，故金人以此为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234323_comment'></div>金人得商州，则与唐、邓声气相接，非但金、洋、均、房不可立，襄阳势必甚孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234323_comment'></div>前日乌陵尚书面出分牒一纸，包裹四至，不明言商州，但云永兴军路，东南至唐、邓，西至秦、凤，南至山南不系永兴军路州郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234323_comment'></div>问之，则曰永兴军路乃商州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234323_comment'></div>如此，则于均、房、金、洋凡在山南郡县皆有妨碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234323_comment'></div>再三商议，不肯改换。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234323_comment'></div>臣须具奏取旨，遂取去公牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234323_comment'></div>秦州在渭南，而地势与河特侵渭北，熙河反出其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234323_comment'></div>金人不得秦州，则与泾原诸路相隔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234323_comment'></div>朝廷无秦州，则阶、成、岷、凤外无屏蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234323_comment'></div>但以轻重较之，金人于秦利害为重，在朝廷为稍轻尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234323_comment'></div>此三处无一可与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234323_comment'></div>臣缘和议大计已定，北官自铁山以西，旋次裁减，十去五六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234323_comment'></div>如成、凤等处，皆已差知州随行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234323_comment'></div>今所欲三处，确然不肯商议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234323_comment'></div>度其势，未可遽回，故欲且与具奏，续为陛下计之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234323_comment'></div>而北官强臣交割退兵，臣不敢从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234323_comment'></div>若朝廷径遣人赴军前求之，皆尚有说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234323_comment'></div>北官谓商州时侵出山北，与南山不齐，不可立界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234323_comment'></div>然自长安南入容道，尚二百里方及商州，自商州，又山行百里至丰阳，丰阳百里至上津，乃今商州移治去处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234323_comment'></div>朝廷必不得已，取商州旧治捐与之，而以丰阳为界，则门户犹半存也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234323_comment'></div>秦州旧城已废，今乃新筑小垒，势苟不能，皆全捐以与之，求贷和尚原为藩篱，恐或可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234323_comment'></div>如其不然，少增岁赂以赎之亦可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234323_comment'></div>此外，臣不知其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234323_comment'></div>异时吴玠固尝失此，然出于一时仓卒，金人暂得之后，由和议旋亦舍去，勿谓曩尝失而无深患也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1234323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年2月27日</a>　郑刚中与左中大夫、四川转运判官兼宣抚使参谋官李觀与金使分画地界。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年3月</a>　胡世将卒于仙人关，托事于郑刚中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年5月</a>　夏，除端明殿学士、川陕宣抚副使，兼营田，转左朝奉郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年5月</a>　除端明殿学士、川陕宣抚副使，兼营田，转左朝奉郎。作品：《除端明殿学士奏》<div id='poem_1234324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除端明殿学士奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234324")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234324'>臣窃以朝廷以上流为重，上流以陕、蜀为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234324_comment'></div>虽邻国通和，兵甲不用，然取百郡之赋，馈十万之师，惟安靖不扰，渐与图为休息，然后可以上宽西顾，非轻责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234324_comment'></div>顾臣何人，辄当此选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234324_comment'></div>崇资峻职，复畀付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234324_comment'></div>臣欲尽沥肝胆，极恳固避，则军无主帅，事已留积，帝阍万里，何日可闻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234324_comment'></div>臣除将宣抚司职事已行管干外，所有转三官并端明殿学士恩命，伏望圣慈特赐寝罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234324_comment'></div>选德望威名著立者，倚分一面之忧，然后为称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234324_comment'></div>臣无任皇惧激切恳祈之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1234324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年6月</a>　郑刚中奉命出使西方与金划分地界。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年7月</a>　上令郑处置吴璘招卫兵事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月</a>　金使持书求和尚原、方山原等地。郑刚中等认为和尚原自绍兴四年后，便系刘豫管守，合割大金，从之。是月，遣郑刚中分画交割地界事。郑遣杨从仪、王彦、范宁之等分割地界。<br /></div>
-----end

四川
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年12月</a>　郑请并茶马司入川司管干，减免虚设官职，上从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　是岁陕西连岁不雨，至是泾渭皆竭，秦民无食，争入蜀，刚中以誓书所约，不敢纳，民多散去饿死。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　冬，遇太母回銮恩，转左朝散郎，进爵子，食邑六百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年12月</a>　乞併减秦茶司。作品：《乞併减秦茶司奏》<div id='poem_1234331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_1234331_comment'></div>秦茶司自复置以来，未尝一到，诚为虚设，欲并入川司管干，所有官吏，并随司减罢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1234331_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　与黄魁有书信来往。作品：《回肇庆倅黄魁》<span class='inlineComment2'>（据《回肇庆倅黄魁》中“越辛酉，出使西南，又明年留师”之句疑作于本年。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　跋张景修诗卷。作品：《跋张大夫景修诗卷》<div id='poem_1234623' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234623' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234623")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234623_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234623'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234623'>某少年时，闻毗陵有先生，以诗名而不得见，即今卷中姓名是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234623_comment'></div>宣和壬寅，识先生之子寺丞君于南昌郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234623_comment'></div>又二十年，见先生之遗墨于小轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234623_comment'></div>玩笔力之遒劲，咏句法之中和，薰然慈仁，如对君子。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年2月</a>　奏相度茶马两司应副钱物。作品：《相度茶马两司应副钱物奏》<div id='poem_1234332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>相度茶马两司应副钱物奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十三年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234332")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234332'>奉旨相度茶马两司每年应副都转运司钱物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234332_comment'></div>今相度，乞将成都府路提刑转运司合桩坊场鼓铸食茶税钱三色，共三十二万缗，令都运司径行取拨外，更那融续添钱八万缗，通作四十万缗，并取博马缗一万八千七百五十匹，自绍兴十二年为头应副。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1234332_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年3月</a>　郑刚中乞增印钱引四百万缗，许之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年5月</a>　郑刚中节制诸将极其尊严。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年8月</a>　郑刚中献黄金万两，上谓秦桧曰，顷年张浚尝献金五百镒，是时有余财。卿可谕刚中有余则进，若率于民不可也。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　有隐退之意。作品：《答柴倅元章》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　冬，以年劳转左朝请郎，遇郊恩，进爵伯，食邑九百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年2月</a>　郑刚中奏减民间科须数目，上闻之颇喜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年3月30日</a>　任四川宣抚副使。作品：《甲子春晴久三月晦得频雨喜而为二绝句》<div id='poem_174444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲子春晴久三月晦得频雨喜而为二绝句<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年3月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174444")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174444'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174444'>夜半风雷破久晴，四檐侵晓尚泠泠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174444_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174444'>欣然拥被重寻睡，梦见汉中春麦青。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174444_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174444'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174444_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174445?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年3月30日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174445'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174445'>春晚郁蒸如溽暑，朝来萧飒似清秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174445_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174445'>千山雨后阴云凝，三日楼前野水流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174445_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174445'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年6月26日</a>　减四川和糴米一年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年7月</a>　作《思耕亭记》<div id='poem_1234666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思耕亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234666")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234666'>绍兴十二年十二月，上命川陕宣抚司自河池移治利州，示休息兵革、裁省用度之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234666_comment'></div>本路转运判官、兼权知利州事王陟，乃移治城南，虚其郡舍而宣抚使居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234666_comment'></div>舍在城之西北隅，有亭名「清晖」，筑于城上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234666_comment'></div>郡山东，嘉陵江峻洁于其前，亭盖以是名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234666_comment'></div>岁月久深，榜目已废，规模冗陋，土木垂压，转运公治而起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234666_comment'></div>某一日置酒其上，会宾幕，问曰：「兹亭新矣，吾以『思耕』易其故号，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234666_comment'></div>客疑而进曰：「是于亭何义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234666_comment'></div>且强而仕，老而休，一犁谷口之云，于公岂不甚乐！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234666_comment'></div>然公方为上经理西南，斯民日几阜康，不思以此报政，而归耕之思乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234666_comment'></div>某曰：「噫嘻，岂为是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234666_comment'></div>览长江之险，思营田之利，予实有感于斯亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234666_comment'></div>夫嘉陵之源发于凤之大散，旁由故镇，缭绕渔关，循崖而出，力未能载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234666_comment'></div>自渔关下武兴，浮三泉，南流二百六十里至于亭下，又顺流踰剑入阆，东走安汉，疾趋于合之汉初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234666_comment'></div>已则会东西二川，并势望夔峡之道，争门而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234666_comment'></div>回视渔关，不知其高几里，皆终岁漕饷之所浮，水既不得平流，皆因地而浅深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234666_comment'></div>自滟滪逆数至渔关之药水，号名滩者六百有奇，石之虎伏兽奔者，又崎岖杂乱于诸滩之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234666_comment'></div>米舟相衔，且尽犯险，率破大竹为百丈之篾缆，有力者十百为群，皆负而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234666_comment'></div>滩怒水激，号呼相应，却立不得前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234666_comment'></div>有如竹断舟退，其遇石而碎，与汩俱入者，皆蜀人之脂膏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234666_comment'></div>小人恃有此，颇复盗用官米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234666_comment'></div>度赃厚罪大，则凿舟沈之，岁陷刑辟与籍入亡家者，亦累而有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234666_comment'></div>故漕粟之及渔关者，计所亡失常十二，吾然后知田之不可不耕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234666_comment'></div>武侯以草庐素定之画，频年兵出，皆以食尽而归，则西南漕饷之艰，盖千古矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234666_comment'></div>吾君诚心善邻，边鄙不耸，命中外以宽厚之泽荡洗烦苛，塞卒十万，今皆櫜弓捲甲而卧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234666_comment'></div>吾诚能借其馀力，杂耕关外，率以平岁缦田为准，不计狼戾，第得粟一钟，即减漕粟三钟之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234666_comment'></div>俟诸营储食，能如晁错所谓足支五岁，则时赦农租，当下天子之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234666_comment'></div>凡此，皆某临流之所深念者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234666_comment'></div>宾幕闻而称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234666_comment'></div>某曰：「谓吾言善，则愿与公等勉之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234666_comment'></div>绍兴十四年七月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1234666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年9月</a>　乞分利州路为两路。作品：《乞分利州路为两路奏》<div id='poem_1234334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞分利州路为两路奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234334")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234334'>今措置，欲将利州路分作东西两路，内吴璘乞差充利州西路安抚使，以阶、成、西和、凤、兴、文、龙州隶属；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234334_comment'></div>杨政乞差充利州东路安抚使，以兴元府、洋、利、阆、巴、蓬、剑州、大安军隶属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234334_comment'></div>郭浩所带理合一体，今欲除落「经略」二字，乞以金房开达州安抚使为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234334_comment'></div>知成州王彦、知阶州姚仲、知西和州程俊、知凤州杨从仪所带沿边安抚及管内安抚，并合除落。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1234334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年10月</a>　自编《北山中集》完成作序。作品：《北山集序》<div id='poem_1234615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北山集叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234615")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234615'>《北山初集》，即余所谓《笑腹编》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234615_comment'></div>余以绍兴乙卯至甲子岁所录文字，自号《北山中集》，《笑腹编》则宣和卒丑至乙卯岁中所录者，因号《初集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234615_comment'></div>若辛丑以前见于纸笔者，皆为盗所火，不复能记忆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234615_comment'></div>甲子而后，时时因事有藁，老懒杂置箧中，他日有能为余收拾者否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234615_comment'></div>所未能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234615_comment'></div>绍兴甲子十月日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1234615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1234615'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北山文集》卷首，影印文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1234615_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年10月</a>　太后生辰，郑言会边事宁息，除军政不可待报者，且从便宜指挥外，其有格法事，立收还省部。作品：《格法事收还省部奏》<div id='poem_1234333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>格法事收还省部奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十四年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234333")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234333'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234333'>今边事宁息，除军政不可待报者且从便宜指挥外，其有格法事，并收还省部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234333_comment'></div>吏、刑部请除文武臣僚磨勘、封赠、酬赏、叙复、章服、奏荐，及诸州应奏谳狱案外，令本司照前后指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1234333_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年10月</a>　刚中族兄郑濬妻子归葬。作品：《族嫂陈氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1234689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>族嫂陈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234689")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234689'>某族有兄讳浚，字资深，世居婺之金华，故中散公讳详之孙，故知录公讳汝嘉之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234689_comment'></div>宣和辛丑，东浙盗平，某还自外邑，资深已下世，族人凋零破坏，无家不孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234689_comment'></div>资深之夫人方卧病，指其子琯辈为某哭且言曰：「兄不幸，枉祸之馀，独四男子，敢以累叔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234689_comment'></div>傥诗书义理之言，时开道之，他日为家为学，仅立门户，获盖前人之大痛，所以友兄之谊高矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234689_comment'></div>某闻而叹曰：「嫂志如是，资深之业，其忧不昌乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234689_comment'></div>自是，琯与琚者苦志经营，条寻坠绪，力振起之，而镶与琈者，未尝一日不以书卷自随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234689_comment'></div>绍兴壬子，某既登进士第，蒙上委使，十年未得归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234689_comment'></div>闻琯辈各专其业，筑第辟馆，聚书延士，园池花木，庭帏晬温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234689_comment'></div>夫人雍容其间，庄笑言，慎礼则，起居康宁，规矩勤俭，中散公之家世风流如在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234689_comment'></div>岁癸亥七月乙丑，夫人以疾卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234689_comment'></div>明年甲子，琯遣人走益昌，以葬请余铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234689_comment'></div>某曰，夫人之贤，乡里宗族能道之，不铭可传也，至岁月次序，则宜永之金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234689_comment'></div>夫人姓陈氏，同郡赠中奉大夫讳邻臣之女，享年六十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234689_comment'></div>男五人：长曰瑞，先卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234689_comment'></div>次即琯、琚、镶、琈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234689_comment'></div>女六人：长适贡士陈柄，次适进士张𩑰、陈格、陈正己、陈嵃、陈岠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234689_comment'></div>孙男女一十四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234689_comment'></div>以甲子十月二十日葬保福山，合于资深之窆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234689_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1234689'>荥阳中艰，义理其子家再昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234689_comment'></div>若堂之封，壤泉钟聚深且长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234689_comment'></div>有缄铭诗，为琯万里下巴江。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1234689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年10月28日</a>　任左朝请郎。作品：《类试院放榜众论以得士为庆作古诗一章呈详定钱宪元素及同院诸公绍兴甲子十月二十八日也》<div id='poem_174926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>类试院放榜众论以得士为庆作古诗一章呈详定钱宪元素及同院诸公绍兴甲子十月二十八日也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年10月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174926")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174926'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174926'>书生业辞艺，不为觅科举。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174926'>胸中负器识，笔下有今古。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174926'>君看阿房赋，岂是布衣语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174926'>独其在糊名，贵贱惟所主。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174926'>得之类至宝，弃去祗如土。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174926'>有司开化炉，镕铸要精处。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174926'>时方为鼎镛，小冶不应鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174926'>诸公皆名流，学海浩吞吐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174926'>丹灵骨先换，入榜尽龙虎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174926'>访以执文柄，我亦费罗取。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174926'>书生家风寒，仆马在何许。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174926'>趼足赴重围，裹饭坐长庑。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174926'>视公帘幕间，若有霄汉阻。<div id='poem_sentence_12_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_174926'>那知先达心，每事必念祖。<div id='poem_sentence_13_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_174926'>未把短檠弃，尚记灯烛苦。<div id='poem_sentence_14_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_174926'>关防周罅隙，考校到毫缕。<div id='poem_sentence_15_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_174926'>杂置战场文，一字不轻与。<div id='poem_sentence_16_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_174926'>如持古黄钟，端坐分律吕。<div id='poem_sentence_17_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_174926'>在处拔其尤，可但十得五。<div id='poem_sentence_18_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_174926'>奉此贤能书，足以上天府。<div id='poem_sentence_19_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_174926'>蜀士多豪英，父老自能数。<div id='poem_sentence_20_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_174926'>谓或有遗珠，勉使相接武。<div id='poem_sentence_21_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_174926'>我辈酒樽空，边城隔烟雨<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《北山集》卷一二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_22_174926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_174926'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_174926_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　受何榘之托作《何氏考妣墓表》<div id='poem_1234688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何氏考妣墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234688")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234688'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234688'>建炎元年四月丁亥，将仕郎何君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234688_comment'></div>明年正月己酉，葬于邑之同义乡长松坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234688_comment'></div>又明年某月甲子，君之夫人郑氏卒，以其年九月丙午，合葬长松之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234688_comment'></div>绍兴十四年，其子矩致书为某言曰：「矩不孝，并失怙恃，属时多艰，风波靡宁，仅于鞍马之隙，奉二柩藏于土，所谓彰遗德而传后世者，未遑及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234688_comment'></div>念遂湮没，则罪逆之身殒越难报，尚惟论撰世次，发扬幽光，表于墓上，则无穷之恨，万分可塞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234688_comment'></div>乡人刘友端谨状以请：「兄其为我图之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234688_comment'></div>某因念儿时，闻族有姑归义乌何氏，勤俭慎淑，克相其夫，而何氏以昌，即夫人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234688_comment'></div>夫人之贤，盖先公诸父平日所相与称道者，某其敢忘之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234688_comment'></div>君讳先，字谦终，世为婺之义乌人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234688_comment'></div>曾大父湜，大父祐，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234688_comment'></div>父京，亦守将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234688_comment'></div>将仕公生三男，君仲子也，幼子蕡游学蚤死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234688_comment'></div>君与伯兄奉承乃父，经画其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234688_comment'></div>将仕公赋性严毅，智度深峻，而又奋志为生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234688_comment'></div>君独从容启悟，得其欢心，以古人积散取予之道开陈其旁，使贫窭受惠，孤嫠得所，田园自饶，而州里称为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234688_comment'></div>将仕公即世，君则以所以事父者事其兄，恭谨逊顺，发于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234688_comment'></div>相处六十年间，周旋曲折，如手足之不相忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234688_comment'></div>既孝友著闻，门户和气粹然，故凡与君缔结姻好者，皆吾乡之贤士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234688_comment'></div>其居在重峦曲水之间，聚书辟馆，门巷幽雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234688_comment'></div>夫人郑氏具肴醴，延宾客，君得以徜徉萧散，享安逸而广名誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234688_comment'></div>宣和庚子，盗起青溪，朝廷分兵锄治，邻党所在，蟠结牢甚，矩锐然上破贼之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234688_comment'></div>东南平，朝廷命矩以官，人咸谓矩之休显其亲当自此始，不幸君与夫人死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234688_comment'></div>君享年七十，夫人七十，皆以疾终于寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234688_comment'></div>郑为金华大姓，夫人之懿德，幼蔼吾宗，凡君孝友之行终始无缺者，皆其赞助之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234688_comment'></div>君为人简洁方正，寡笑言，平生不事进取，而涉猎经传，谈道今古，得其理义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234688_comment'></div>晚年尤好修塔庙，治津梁，乐施惠，盖其与夫人辈设心在于化人为善，非因感于祸福之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234688_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234688_comment'></div>世之作德者，孰谓无报也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234688_comment'></div>余观何氏自上世绵积，然将仕公三男子，蕡最力学而器业不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234688_comment'></div>君四男子，楶、杲、槃皆先卒，所存者独矩尔，乃能奋布衣取官，今为保义郎，磊落慷慨，未可量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234688_comment'></div>孙男三人：忻、恪、怃，咸积学自进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234688_comment'></div>女一人，适进士陈阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234688_comment'></div>孝友之泽，至今未已，是虽金石之传不在圹中，而邻里称道，自可传于后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234688_comment'></div>惟兹墓上之碑，姑见矩之孝思云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234688_comment'></div>某月某日，乃立石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234688_comment'></div>为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1234688'>长松之原，戊申之阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1234688_comment'></div>惟兹圹中，无金石传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1234688_comment'></div>所传后者，乡党之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1234688_comment'></div>岁越甲子，具此深镌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1234688_comment'></div>长松生风，朝霞暮烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1234688_comment'></div>视我铭诗，何千万年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1234688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　夏，除资政殿学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年5月</a>　奏乞降处分减对籴量米。作品：《乞降处分减对籴量米奏》<div id='poem_1234335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞降处分减对籴粮米奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十五年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234335")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234335'>欲减成都府路对籴粮米一十二万石，潼川府路六万石，切虑两路州县却将已前积年欠负驱催，或以那兑别色斛斗支遣拨还为名，复行搔扰，甚非宽恤之意，伏望特降处分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1234335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年10月</a>　刚中忤秦桧，秦桧不欲刚中掌利权，使人奏请四川宣抚司置总领一司，掌管财赋。削弱郑刚中权利。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年11月</a>　秦桧疑郑刚中，荐赵不弃，赵行太府少卿，充四川宣抚司总领馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年7月</a>　赵不弃欲尽取宣抚司所储，郑刚中不与，赵不弃怒，劾刚中亲信王陟。刚中愬于朝，不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　冬，以年劳转左朝奉大夫，遇郊恩，进爵郡侯，食邑一千二百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年12月</a>　刚中奏减两川米脚钱三十二万缗，激赏钱二万匹，许之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年1月</a>　友曹宏归葬。作品：《右承议郎致仕曹公墓志》<div id='poem_1234690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右承议郎致仕曹公墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234690")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234690'>某族叔千之，名士也，以女归同郡曹毅君佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234690_comment'></div>尝怪君佐以田家改业为太学士，而士夫之贤者乐与之游，是必有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234690_comment'></div>识者曰：「君佐之学，盖其兄安雅公实畀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234690_comment'></div>安雅辛苦治生，生事理，则请其父买书择师教其弟，又教其子绩，曹之白屋改矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234690_comment'></div>政和丙申，某游乡校，绩为同舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234690_comment'></div>明年绩贡辟廱，又明年中上舍高选，自是名宦益振，而安雅教子功成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234690_comment'></div>绍兴癸亥，公随绩官益昌，越乙丑二月十九日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234690_comment'></div>绩奉丧归葬如礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234690_comment'></div>前期以左朝奉议、前知渠州流江县事练祗柔之状，泣血请铭，谊其可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234690_comment'></div>公讳宏，字安雅，世为婺之金华人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234690_comment'></div>曾祖光明，祖欢，父享，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234690_comment'></div>安雅天性孝友，遇人诚信和易，喜愠不形于色，乡党钦爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234690_comment'></div>君佐虽未第而死，然绩已成立，诸孙相次进，茂颍者复自湖北漕司荐送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234690_comment'></div>安雅知门户儒学之风不衰，则围棋饮酒，所在自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234690_comment'></div>方某之宣谕四川也，请于朝，以绩偕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234690_comment'></div>及被旨留师，欲请主管机宜，绩曰：「愿归从老人问行止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234690_comment'></div>至则安雅欣然随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234690_comment'></div>谓所亲曰：「顾夷险，择远近，非吾望子孙意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234690_comment'></div>自入蜀，遇峻阪辄下马，行步如飞，左右者趋之莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234690_comment'></div>居益昌且二年，每相过，必叙说乡曲，持杯笑语，尽醉而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234690_comment'></div>一日，忽令绩寄谢知友，治后事，家人惊勿敢听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234690_comment'></div>翌旦，正衣冠，翛然逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234690_comment'></div>呜呼贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234690_comment'></div>安雅六被恩封，官至右承议郎，享年八十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234690_comment'></div>娶章氏，五男子：绩今官至左朝奉郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234690_comment'></div>曰纲者，蚤卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234690_comment'></div>曰缙、曰总、曰绍，悉知愿守家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234690_comment'></div>女二人：长适胡璿，次适其从弟琏，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234690_comment'></div>孙男女二十六人，曾孙男女一十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234690_comment'></div>以丁卯正月壬午葬于所居之乡万家坞，合章夫人之竁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234690_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1234690'>惟公种德，自其父祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234690_comment'></div>公有子弟，自公学古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234690_comment'></div>学古而修，坐观成效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234690_comment'></div>安荣寿考，亦享其报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234690_comment'></div>幽幽壤泉，郁郁松柏，万家之坞，藏此诗曰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1234690_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
郴州
-----detail

-----title

-----title
天门
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='32c6e34b2a584c92a13ca5a4716df4bf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("32c6e34b2a584c92a13ca5a4716df4bf");'><span id='32c6e34b2a584c92a13ca5a4716df4bf_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　责授濠州团练副使，复州安置。作品：《马伏波请征蛮据鞍矍铄时年六十一陆鸿渐景陵人早年事比丘后始改业为儒今复州东门外小寺断碑犹言是鸿渐当时授业院也予去年蒙恩谪桂阳正年六十一今徙复州当访鸿渐之遗踪戏成一绝》<div id='poem_174808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174808?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_2_174808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年2月</a>　刚中在湖北停留听旨候命。作品：《荆州之川曰江曰汉曰沱曰潜曰三虀其泽曰云梦汉志谓三虀在江夏竟陵竟陵即今之景陵复州是也春秋传楚子与郑伯田於江南之梦梦与云自不同渡武昌道汉阳至复州非冬晴水涸则渺漫极目乃三虀之尾所谓梦泽也己己二月春水未生行蒲稗间累日将至景陵望孤城盖大泽中之环堵州治即古章台也》<div id='poem_174928' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174928' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174928?labeling=true' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174928_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174928'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174928'>江气藏空阔，春云压洲渚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174928'>蒲稗迷远目，断续川陆阻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174928'>幽哉沮洳旁，谓是囚伏所。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174928'>十日南窗下，卧听清明雨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174928'>此是古章台，家山在何许。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174928_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174928'></div><div
