-----title
封开
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='391480aa26b54958babc39ac78dfd7ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("391480aa26b54958babc39ac78dfd7ee");'><span id='391480aa26b54958babc39ac78dfd7ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1154')">1149-1154年</a>，62-67岁</div><div id='391480aa26b54958babc39ac78dfd7ee' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年6月</a>　六月自复州徙封州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1151')">1149-1151年</a>　罢职移居封州。作品：《到封州谢表》《经史专音序》《族兄巨中嫂王氏姚氏合葬铭》《左氏九六编序》《达尝编序》《庚午腊中苦寒不雪不雪岭南之常而苦寒为稀有矣》《庚午冬至夜（二首）》《宣和丁酉太夫人终天墓庐中读金光明经见摩诃萨埵投身饲虎因缘尝以颂赞叹之绍兴庚午临封又得是经诵读复成一偈》《三砚记》《记白朱砂》《辛未中春旦极热流汗暮而风雨如深秋》《辛未元夜》《上婺倅王学士以门客牒试书》<div id='poem_1234350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>到封州谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234350")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234350'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234350'>成法难宽，自投宪网；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234350_comment'></div>大君善贷，仰戴仁天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234350_comment'></div>念孤恩至此以何追，虽流涕痛惩而莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234350_comment'></div>亟收危魄，祗拜温词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234350_comment'></div>茫然晨夜以奔趋，惟是寝兴而震悸<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234350_comment'></div>伏念臣桑榆得路，韦布起家，遭逢尽出于圣神，报答不忘于顶踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234350_comment'></div>而臣取穷有道，召福无门，心思暗以皆迷，禄食浮而取败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234350_comment'></div>敢效愚之勿勉，寔体国之未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234350_comment'></div>违戾弥年，含洪有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234350_comment'></div>彼天视履，既招盈满之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234350_comment'></div>惟道平施，宜正偏私之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234350_comment'></div>雷霆所过，斧钺犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234350_comment'></div>陛下以仁为恩，朝廷于帝其训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234350_comment'></div>百愆俱宥，一切优容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234350_comment'></div>全收震曜之威，止从轻典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234350_comment'></div>许集伤残之气，再保庸神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234350_comment'></div>无所糜躯，惟知顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234350_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下功高治古，道契格王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234350_comment'></div>体简易以示人，象著明而在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234350_comment'></div>讫内外不罹于咎，大德日生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234350_comment'></div>无隐微不得其情，容光必照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234350_comment'></div>自诒戚者，亦惟教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234350_comment'></div>致此妄迷，仰蒙全贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234350_comment'></div>臣敢不熏心知惧，伏地省非？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234350_comment'></div>靖惟积沴之身，远倾葵藿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234350_comment'></div>独有再生之赐，难报乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234350_comment'></div>臣无任屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1234350_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>经史专音序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234613")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234613'>凡字书一音者，《韵略》科以四声，各从本韵，用之无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234613_comment'></div>自一音以上，韵辄圈之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234613_comment'></div>附圈者，皆字之有他音者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234613_comment'></div>甚矣，他音之多岐，而专音之易失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234613_comment'></div>后学狃于传诵，初或失真，场屋之间，迫于晷刻，义复不审，往往谓圈字可以通用，而不知六经百氏，固有专读之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234613_comment'></div>误取谬用，所不能免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234613_comment'></div>予病此，近为旁通书，取音一以上，经史有专音及名物定号不相为用者标于上，而以又音系其下，训释可以发明者疏于后，本字外事实可以资益者并载之，盖简而易见，辨而可守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234613_comment'></div>惟是《韵略》音注比《释文》容有不同，而予于圈字，其去取亦各有音，别为《叙例》，附序之后，通号曰《经史专音》，凡五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234613_comment'></div>陆氏有言：书音之用，本示童蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234613_comment'></div>予为是书，考据不能周尽，其于示童子也，庶几焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234613_comment'></div>绍兴十九年十二月日，观如居士序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1234613_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>族兄巨中嫂王氏姚氏合葬铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234683")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234683'>吾兄巨中，讳溥，婺之金华人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234683_comment'></div>宣和辛丑，盗据婺城，二月戊辰掠拱坦，谓巨中郑姓，家世宦学，害之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234683_comment'></div>其妻姚氏衔负祸毒，哭之百日不绝声，以其年五月乙巳卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234683_comment'></div>子玠艰难险苦，嗣立门户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234683_comment'></div>乙巳十二月庚申，始克奉二丧，并迁其所生母巨中始娶王氏之柩，合葬于东阳乡之黄坞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234683_comment'></div>巨中故中散大夫详之孙，故乡贡进士汝能之子，享年四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234683_comment'></div>姚故同郡士人公度之女，享年四十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234683_comment'></div>巨中失王氏，欲不复娶，则念无以事其母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234683_comment'></div>姚亦归故三班奉职廖几道矣，寡居誓守，坚其志而迫于贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234683_comment'></div>巨中闻其在家孝甚，力求妇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234683_comment'></div>姚不得已，执其罍篚，柔顺庄靓，果欢其姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234683_comment'></div>一子曰珌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234683_comment'></div>巨中不能饮酒而喜宾客，非富有而乐施惠，读书能文而不事进取，居今之世，可以为难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234683_comment'></div>王故缙云县尉秉均之女，死今二十有一年，玠以所葬不吉，徙从新卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234683_comment'></div>志虽弗为具载，然克相巨中而成其德者王始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234683_comment'></div>识墓有石，族弟某哭而铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1234683'>惟兹黄坞，松柏之蓊然者，巨中之阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234683_comment'></div>挟堂封而左右者，王姚祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234683_comment'></div>岂若人而无报，吾固知自玠而后，必有学古扬名而慰幽泉者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1234683_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左氏九六编序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234612")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234612'>《左氏》载春秋卜筮颇详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234612_comment'></div>筮之遇《周易》者之卦一十三，变为二十有六，无变者三，论卦体以明事而不由筮得者八，总三十有七卦，蛊凡两书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234612_comment'></div>予志欲集为一书，久而未暇，近乃成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234612_comment'></div>凡卦之见于《左氏》者，各画其所得象，具载事本与筮史之论，其有疑浑，可加臆说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234612_comment'></div>或近世推占之法，似相契验者，辄附会其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234612_comment'></div>仍以八宫分卦，并逐宫之变体先之，共三卷，通号曰《左氏九六编》，庶简而易求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234612_comment'></div>所集成，偶读元凯书，太康元年，自江陵还襄阳，会汲县民有发其界内旧冢者，大得古书，皆科斗文字，藏入秘府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234612_comment'></div>元凯晚得见之，书多杂碎奇怪，惟《周易》及《纪年》，最为分了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234612_comment'></div>又别一卷，纯集《左氏传》卜筮事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234612_comment'></div>上下次第及其文义，皆与《左氏》同，名曰《师春》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234612_comment'></div>师春似是抄集人名，异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234612_comment'></div>予今所作，是乃《师春》之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234612_comment'></div>其人其书，茫然千古之上，疏集同异，不可得而知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234612_comment'></div>绍兴庚午正月日，观如居士序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1234612_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>达尝编序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234614")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234614'>不知病而投药，非药之失，用药之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234614_comment'></div>寒温违性，佐使非宜，此方之失，亦信方之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234614_comment'></div>己巳以来，怜予病者，既分以药，必授以方，所以体朝廷好生之德，保全瘴疠之身，仁亦至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234614_comment'></div>近取所得方集而编之，是皆用而有信，非所谓未达不敢尝者也，因号之曰《达尝编》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234614_comment'></div>绍兴二十年正月日，观如居士序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1234614_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午腊中苦寒不雪不雪岭南之常而苦寒为希有矣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174900")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174900'>檐风动修竹，终夜玉相戛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174900'>晓望山头松，孤瘦冻欲折。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174900'>欣然扫茅亭，准拟看飞雪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174900'>待之既踰时，脚硬冷如铁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174900'>青山全不老，暮雨空凄绝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174900'>岂非地气偏，湿浊旧不泄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174900'>剪水下云来，祗向虚空歇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174900'>今年腊中寒，万口称凛冽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174900'>此是雪先声，荡洗岭南热。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174900'>蜑叟且莫惊，造化无差别。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174900'>会须烟瘴林，都有琪花结。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174900'>草色润如酥，看取焦枯活。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174900'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_174900_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174725?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午冬至夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年12月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174725")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174725_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174725'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174725'>今夜云开北陆风，丈三将到土圭中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174725'>剥穷谁见阴阳妙，来复方知天地功。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174725'>孤坐看灯浑是梦，苍颜被酒不生红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174725'>却怜土俗追时节，言语虽殊意亦同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174725'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174725_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午冬至夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年12月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174519")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174519'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174519'>旋寻村酒不须浓，饮少愁多酒易供。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174519'>灯下一身家万里，今年恰好是三冬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174519'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174519_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_175027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_175027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/175027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣和丁酉太夫人终天墓庐中读金光明经见摩诃萨埵投身饲虎因缘尝以颂赞叹之绍兴庚午临封又得是经诵读复成一偈<span class='inlineComment2'>（前颂见初集）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_175027")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_175027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_175027'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_175027'>虎有爪距，如刀兵利。<div id='poem_sentence_0_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_175027'>佛岂欲人，置身其喙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_175027'>惟见前法，欢喜怖畏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_175027'>猛火销金，观汝难易。<div id='poem_sentence_3_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_175027'>大慈悲父，持戒定慧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_175027'>作汝津梁，无有障蔽。<div id='poem_sentence_5_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_175027'>瞿夷非虎，冤亲无异。<div id='poem_sentence_6_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_175027'>虎七子者，比丘等是。<div id='poem_sentence_7_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_175027'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_175027_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_175027'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北山文集》卷二六。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_175027_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1234668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三砚记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234668")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234668'>笔砚，书生进业之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234668_comment'></div>予自幼年玩之，今六十三矣，砚大槩合记者有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234668_comment'></div>崇宁间，先子挂冠归自长沙，不一年弃诸孤，家四壁立，忍饥为学不敢荒，尝凿坚木用以当砚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234668_comment'></div>一日于败墙土下得折足砚一枚，濯涤视之，盖歙石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234668_comment'></div>纹如瓜子，殆是百年瓦砾间物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234668_comment'></div>由是携入举场，踰二纪，大小凡百试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234668_comment'></div>绍兴壬子，以奉大对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234668_comment'></div>所谓悲欢穷泰，未尝一日废其用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234668_comment'></div>后省亲旁邑，弗以偕行，偶里中盗起，居人窜伏，还则砚亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234668_comment'></div>逮乙卯官永嘉，或贻以紫莲叶琢，小而肉薄，谓是观音石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234668_comment'></div>石初出永嘉，而知者犹少，质比端溪之良润微不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234668_comment'></div>丁巳以后之省之寺，游秘馆，登曲台，奏论<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1234668", 1234668, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>订议</span>，无不与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234668_comment'></div>辛酉冬，相随使西方，至房陵，卧病邮亭中，濒死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234668_comment'></div>后虽得生，恍惚健忘，砚失所在，予亦留帅坤维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234668_comment'></div>越己亥，又得武昌陶砚，状如风字，宜墨可意，不减前二者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234668_comment'></div>或诮以爱惜过厚，予曰：「适用者贵，唐贤所用大率皆陶也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234668_comment'></div>檄置兵伍，书判刑杀，应对酬酢，偕在边尘间者首尾六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234668_comment'></div>丁卯冬奏事，道次武昌，以曩恶暴著，上宽恩令，食奉祠禄于桂阳，又与偕往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234668_comment'></div>戊辰秋，因事复遗失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234668_comment'></div>自桂阳移景陵，由景陵南至岭外，二年间虽无文字可用，而笔墨遂无所归赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234668_comment'></div>近又得一焉，名曰「玉斗」，众谓下岩佳品，而予不能辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234668_comment'></div>呜呼，孰谓得丧去来无数也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234668_comment'></div>折足之歙以盗亡，永嘉之莲以病亡，武昌之陶以事亡，予累砚耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234668_comment'></div>砚负予耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234668_comment'></div>顾今老矣，为「玉斗」者，止用以疏《周易》，写《维摩经》，不敢极汝用以磷汝德，能与予相终始乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234668_comment'></div>误坠而毁，予当惩元宾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234668_comment'></div>弃予而往，汝亦勿有三砚之负。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1234668_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记白朱砂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234674")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234674'>封有民郭生者，病寒瘴，治久不愈，气血凋耗，日覆重衾，压以铜钱五千重，仅免振掉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234674_comment'></div>室中无昼夜然火，不知温，盖垂死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234674_comment'></div>有道士过，投丹一粒，不移时，病者令彻钱不用，又少顷去火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234674_comment'></div>翌旦再饵一粒，起而食饮如常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234674_comment'></div>或问药于道士，道士曰：「此白朱砂也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234674_comment'></div>「方可得乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234674_comment'></div>道士笑而不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234674_comment'></div>予去年来自湖北，随行僮三人，瘴杀其二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234674_comment'></div>馀一人汪举，虽脱命鬼手，然毒沴不去，气血之枯，大率与封民无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234674_comment'></div>宛转从道士得一粒，亲手投之，踰夕而苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234674_comment'></div>太守赵公元信，一日欣然谓予曰：「道士肯以方授我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234674_comment'></div>如方治药，药成，吾家有喘满病弥年者，试以投之，喘随药定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234674_comment'></div>欲再煅一炉，愿得公證明」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234674_comment'></div>予许之而往观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234674_comment'></div>自旦起火，抵暮火尽，鼎冷药色如雪，相与滴水成圆，若珠玉之走槃，又经数火，益晶明可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234674_comment'></div>呜呼异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234674_comment'></div>元信处心忠厚，视人疾病如痛在其身，今得其方甚真，岂天以活人之功畀之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234674_comment'></div>虽然，世固多异病，亦未尝无良药，药当病，则足以起人死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234674_comment'></div>良药误投，亦可以伤人之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234674_comment'></div>愿公秘方慎与，凡与之药者，必告之曰：「汝所苦如封民，则吾之药为司命矣」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1234674_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛未中春旦极热流汗暮而风雨如深秋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174501")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174501'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174501'>起来流汗对朝曦，暮雨如秋意转迷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174501'>信是岭南秋半景，不须榕叶乱莺啼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174501'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_174501'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_174501_0'>⑴ 自注：柳子厚有春半如秋意转迷，及榕叶满庭莺乱啼之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_174501_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_174880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛未元夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174880")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174880'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174880'>轻寒拥山城，远绿生春草。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174880'>迎神乐元夜，笑语闻蛮獠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174880'>惟有团圆月，报我时节好。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174880'>寸灯岂为孤，卮酒未为少。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174880'>微醺短檠旁，人静茅屋小。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174880'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_174880_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上婺倅王学士以门客牒试书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234356")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234356'>昔柳子厚谓东祠有浮图，病蹩者十年矣，扶服舆曳，羞愧侧匿，已为废人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234356_comment'></div>会里中诸释以经律授人者悉以故去，其徒无所取法，相与谋曰：「蹩师有道，可出而事之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234356_comment'></div>乃盥濯扶持，献巾馈食，浮图遂有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234356_comment'></div>中厩有马驹，病颡者十年矣，垂首披耳，悬涎属地，已为废马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234356_comment'></div>会刺史至，他马痹狭短小，厩人恐不足以授辔，相与谋曰：「病驹有相，可秣饰之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234356_comment'></div>乃浴剔搔剪，刮恶除洟，马驹遂见用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234356_comment'></div>某自礼部退黜之后，病穷亦十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234356_comment'></div>坎𡒄憔悴，苦险顿挫，已为废士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234356_comment'></div>比蒙阁下抆拭提携，收置门下，人皆谓遭遇之势正与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234356_comment'></div>每观断简遗编，未尝不捧持再拜，涕泣横落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234356_comment'></div>庄子谓流人去国之久，往往见似人而喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234356_comment'></div>阁下至润之名，实由苏出，可谓似之者矣，故某尤以遭遇为可喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234356_comment'></div>子厚又谓士之显宠贵剧，则其受赐于人也，无德心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234356_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234356_comment'></div>彼必曰：「我力能得之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234356_comment'></div>是其所出者大，而报其必细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234356_comment'></div>穷厄困辱，则感激捧戴，万万有加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234356_comment'></div>是其所出者小，而报也必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234356_comment'></div>某今日受门下知，其感激捧戴，必将有加矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234356_comment'></div>未能图报，姑借子厚起废之说，为堂下拜谢之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234356_comment'></div>冒浼，不胜恐惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山文集》卷四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234356_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1234356'>与：疑当作「兴」，或「与」下脱「此类」二字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1234356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年1月1日</a>　著《周易窥馀》作品：《周易窥馀序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（郑《周易窥馀序》曰：“予自幼年玩之，今六十三矣。”故系于此年。）</span><div id='poem_1234611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周易窥馀序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234611")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234611'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234611'>《窥馀》，窥窃《易》家馀意，缀缉而成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234611_comment'></div>老来心志凋落健忘，自觉所学渐次遗失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234611_comment'></div>恐他时儿童辈有问，寖就荒唐无以对，故取平时所诵今昔《易》学与意会者，辄次第编录，时自省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234611_comment'></div>此《窥馀》之所为作、所为名、序之所为缕缕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234611_comment'></div>伏羲氏画八卦，古无异论，至重卦则指名不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234611_comment'></div>郑康成辈谓神农，孙盛谓大禹，史迁、扬雄谓文王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234611_comment'></div>攻为神农之说者曰：「耒耨之利，日中之市，固已取诸《益》、取诸《噬嗑》，岂应后来方重卦」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234611_comment'></div>神农之说破，则盛以下自当无语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234611_comment'></div>孔颖达、王弼又谓伏羲氏始用蓍，十有八变而成卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1234611_comment'></div>观变之数，则用蓍犹在六爻之后，造书契以代结绳之治，而书契之作，取诸《益》，重卦者非伏羲乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1234611_comment'></div>伏羲氏画卦，又为重卦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1234611_comment'></div>文王为卦下之辞，又分上下经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1234611_comment'></div>孔子为十翼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1234611_comment'></div>周公为爻辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1234611_comment'></div>此《易纬》所谓三圣人，而周公不与者，周公本文考之志而为之，举文王则知周公之圣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1234611_comment'></div>颖达既坚守弼论不移，后之立异相可否者犹未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1234611_comment'></div>要是指擿相胜，无明白證据，当以王、孔为允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1234611_comment'></div>复有疑者曰：爻辞亦文王所作，非周公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1234611_comment'></div>此盖不考《明夷》尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1234611_comment'></div>文在羑里，无自谓文王之理，亦不得先谓箕子为《明夷》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1234611_comment'></div>韩宣子适鲁见《易象》，云「吾乃知周公之德」，则公作爻辞何疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1234611_comment'></div>马融、陆绩皆知此意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1234611_comment'></div>《系辞》曰：「知者观《彖辞》，则思过半矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1234611_comment'></div>又曰：「圣人设卦观象，系辞焉而明吉凶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1234611_comment'></div>遂又疑夫子不应自赞如此，《彖》、《系》必文王所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1234611_comment'></div>曾不知卦下之辞，乃文王所系，其所系辞亦可谓之《彖》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1234611_comment'></div>夫子于上下《系》特赞序之，与夫子所为《彖辞》自不相碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1234611_comment'></div>范谔昌误疑《乾·彖》与《文言》重复，而谓文王为《彖》者，亦此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1234611_comment'></div>至于十翼之目，亦复纷纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1234611_comment'></div>以《彖》、《象》、《系辞》三者各分上下，而与《文言》、《序卦》、《说卦》、《杂卦》四篇号为十者，颖达主之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1234611_comment'></div>以《彖》也，大小《象》也，上下《系辞》也，乾、坤《文言》也，而与《序卦》、《说卦》、《杂卦》三篇号为十者，胡旦主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1234611_comment'></div>以《象》分大小，而不以《彖》分上下，旦说为胜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1234611_comment'></div>以《文言》分乾、坤，似未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1234611_comment'></div>去古远矣，学者要当以意所安者为是，故两存之，以俟来哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1234611_comment'></div>通乎此，然后可以读《易》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1234611_comment'></div>或问曰：「子为书，始《屯》、《蒙》，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1234611_comment'></div>曰：「予于《乾》、《坤》，不敢谈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1234611_comment'></div>《易》者，天地万物之奥，《乾》、《坤》则又《易》之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1234611_comment'></div>圣人妙《易》书之神而藏之《乾》、《坤》，其所示人者，犹委曲载之《文言》，孰谓学者可以一言定乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1234611_comment'></div>尊《乾》、《坤》而不敢论，自《屯》、《蒙》而往，以象求爻，因爻识卦，万有一见其彷佛，则随子索母，沿流寻源，《乾》《坤》之微，或可得而探也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1234611_comment'></div>今固未敢妄有窥焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1234611_comment'></div>又问：「《易》曰商瞿子木亲受业夫子，下抵汉魏，专门名家者不胜计，虽互有得失之论，大槩不过象、义二者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1234611_comment'></div>就其意趣不合最甚者，惟李鼎祚、王弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1234611_comment'></div>其专用象变三十馀家，而不足义者，鼎祚也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1234611_comment'></div>尽扫象变，不用古注，而专以意训者，弼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1234611_comment'></div>子为书，为象乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1234611_comment'></div>为义乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1234611_comment'></div>曰：「有象则有义，以义训者，不可以遗象也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1234611_comment'></div>义不由象出，是犹终日论影，而不知形之所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1234611_comment'></div>偏于一而废其一，学者所以难，予《窥馀》所不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1234611_comment'></div>近世程颐正叔尝为《易传》，朱震子发又为《集传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1234611_comment'></div>二书颇相弥缝于象义之间，其于发古今之奥为有功焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1234611_comment'></div>但《易》之道广大变通，诸家不能以一辞尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1234611_comment'></div>有可窥之馀，吾则兼而取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1234611_comment'></div>杜预《春秋经传集解后序》，载晋太康元年，汲县发旧冢，大得古书，皆科斗文字，不可训知，独《周易》及《纪年》，最为分了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1234611_comment'></div>《周易》上下篇，与今正同，而无《彖》、《象》、《文言》、《系辞》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1234611_comment'></div>预疑于时仲尼造之于鲁，尚未播之远国，而《汉艺文志》「《易经》十二篇」，谓上下经及十翼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1234611_comment'></div>以是考之，汉之《易》已十二篇，但经与十翼自为篇秩，非若今《易》之各附卦爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1234611_comment'></div>先儒谓费直专以《彖》、《象》、《文言》参解《易》爻，谓王辅嗣《象》本释经，欲相附近，故辞与《象》，各附于当爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1234611_comment'></div>要之取古本辄相分合，二子不容无过，然圣人之旨未大悖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1234611_comment'></div>并见于序之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1234611_comment'></div>绍兴壬申正月旦，观如居士山斋书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1234611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年1月15日</a>　罢职移居封州。作品：《壬申年封州自正旦连雨至元宵不止城中泥沼没骭而人家犹烧灯也》《壬申年封州自正旦雨至元宵不止》（人图作元夜）《壬申年封州自正旦雨至元宵不止》（江风侵山云不干）<div id='poem_174424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬申年封州自正旦连雨至元宵不止城中泥淖没骭而人家犹烧灯也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174424")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174424'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174424'>山城泥淖裹人家，雨脚连绵更似麻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174424'>元夜何妨灯数点，污渠合是有莲花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174424'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174424_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬申年封州自正旦雨至元宵不止</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174813")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174813'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174813'>人图作元夜，剪纱累红莲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174813'>天欲下膏泽，万瓦飞流泉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174813'>烧灯雨何损，不过市井喧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174813'>春若无此雨，从谁觅丰年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174813'>痴儿騃女临管弦，见雨不止意缺然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174813'>百千灯光祗照夜，山下一犁知几钱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174813'>人间万事有轻重，况是作止当从天。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174813_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174813'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_174813_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬申年封州自正旦雨至元宵不止</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174680")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174680'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174680'>江风<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作涨）</span>侵山云不乾，迎春送腊雨漫漫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174680'>勾萌潜识化工意，泥淖莫嗟行路难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174680'>闭户定无元夜醉，拥衾如对九秋寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174680'>池塘烟草弄风日，此景当从晴后看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174680'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　罢职移居封州，子良嗣来封州祝寿。作品：《良嗣壬申年来为生朝寿作一诗答之》<div id='poem_174878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>良嗣壬申年来为生朝寿作一诗答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174878")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174878'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174878'>惟吾始生朝，汝祖五十八。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174878'>甫及贾谊少，祖易大夫箦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174878'>怀绷至不天，能有几岁月。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174878'>不得著斑衣，惨惨意常缺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174878'>吾如汝祖年，汝已双髻茁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174878'>似我蒲伏岁，汝方事绅笏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174878'>我更得祖寿，尚有十年活。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174878'>汝之事亲日，加我一陪阔。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174878'>其如父与子，灾福势相轧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174878'>灾胜福力微，万罪如箭发。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174878'>向非天地恩，谁肉两躯骨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174878'>后效皆渺茫，前愆正磨刮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174878'>今兹各天涯，瘴水东西隔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_174878'>汝作飞云感，我类寸<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>肠割。<div id='poem_sentence_13_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_174878'>天之加汝者，如与复如夺。<div id='poem_sentence_14_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_174878'>每见榴花红，为汝惜时节。<div id='poem_sentence_15_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_174878'>手持祝生香，自向炉中热。<div id='poem_sentence_16_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_174878'>但愿早团栾，盘餐共粗粝。<div id='poem_sentence_17_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_174878'>将此离别数，造物为除豁。<div id='poem_sentence_18_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_174878'>小宽寒暑期，未作枯木折。<div id='poem_sentence_19_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_174878'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_174878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_174878'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_174878_0'>⑴ 原作杏，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_174878_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1154')">1152-1154年</a>　罢职移居封州。作品：《与董梧州彦明》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《与董梧州彦明》文曰：“绍兴壬子，廷唱既出，大雨无具……今二十年，不谓犹以囚罪之身……”知作于此年。）</span>《拟送傅推官吉先予以绍兴己巳六月自复徙封，吉先后一月到任》《癸酉年梅花开已逾数月而窗外黄菊方烂然》《癸酉中冬四日江行》《别方安抚》（伏审光膺宸命）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《别方安抚》（伏审光膺宸命）文中言病重，自感时日无多。疑作于郑刚中去世之前，姑系于此年。）</span>《别方安抚》（某自正月二日感瘴病）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《别方安抚》（某自正月二日感瘴病）文中言病重，自感时日无多。疑作于郑刚中去世之前，姑系于此年。）</span>《别方稚川》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《别方稚川》文中言病重，自感时日无多。疑作于郑刚中去世之前，姑系于此年。）</span>《答袁教授》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《答袁教授》文中言病重，自感时日无多。疑作于郑刚中去世之前，姑系于此年。）</span><div id='poem_174708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟送傅推官吉先予以绍兴己巳六月自复徙封吉先后一月到任</a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174708")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_174708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174708'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174708'>漂流忆昨到封川，相继人看渌水莲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174708'>屈指君犹成一任，过头吾已出三年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174708'>款门对坐惟棋局，判袂论情付酒船。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174708'>九月秋风去帆疾，可能相望不依然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174708'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_174708_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸酉年梅花开已踰月而窗<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作门）</span>外黄菊方烂然</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174551")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_174551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174551'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174551'>江梅久矣报涂粉，篱菊傲然方铸金。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174551'>岭外四时惟一气，难分冬雾与秋阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174551'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_174551_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_174922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_174922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/174922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸酉中冬四日江行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年11月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_174922")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_174922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_174922'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_174922'>新寒荡馀暑，小雨结离愁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_174922'>行人向西去，江水自东流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_174922'>我趁孤船归，回肠车万周。<div id='poem_sentence_2_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_174922'>假寐桨声中，清梦何悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_174922'>恍若傅两翼，飘然得浮游。<div id='poem_sentence_4_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_174922'>仙风入山骨，佳气遮林邱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_174922'>尘外人物古，云间楼殿幽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_174922'>自念此何许，而容区中囚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_174922'>旁有老人笑，谓予失初谋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_174922'>贪前慕垂饵，遂为香所钩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_174922'>今兹穷瘁身，抱病炎荒陬。<div id='poem_sentence_10_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_174922'>终岁骨肉念，百年离合忧。<div id='poem_sentence_11_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_174922'>俛默事迎送，嗟嗟亦良羞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_174922'>予欲从之拜，江波拍船头。<div id='poem_sentence_13_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_174922'>危坐记惝恍，熏心省愆尤。<div id='poem_sentence_14_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_174922'>玉玷容可磨，水跌那许收。<div id='poem_sentence_15_174922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_174922'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_174922_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别方安抚<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234566")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234566'>伏审光膺宸命，移镇近藩，地与望隆，宠随恩重，伏惟欢庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234566_comment'></div>某正兹卧病，尚阻修诚，更辱移书，惟知负愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234566_comment'></div>念旌麾之已远，攀履舄以无从，感恋之私，毫楮难尽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1234566_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234567?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234567'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234567'>某自正月二日感瘴病，中闻新除，欣喜至于体轻，但欲略拜区区，亦不能成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234567_comment'></div>止俟安健，而日复一日，病势有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234567_comment'></div>今踰七十日，又旬馀不喜食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234567_comment'></div>二月间，自罗池买得杉木四片，已治周身之具，虽未至昏迷，而皮骨自觉无神矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234567_comment'></div>托芘之久，语离之遽，怀此高谊，虽言何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234567_comment'></div>傥或未至颠仆，不知他时尚容修记犯门阑否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234567_comment'></div>自馀惟为远业善保重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1234567_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别方稚川</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234568")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234568'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234568'>某三年之间，无一字至记室者，岂自疏哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234568_comment'></div>度不可故已尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234568_comment'></div>忽辱坠书，既感且慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234568_comment'></div>伏承阁学移镇近藩，联舟北去，棣华光映，何庆如之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234568_comment'></div>某托芘之久，孤踪有依，今遽一涯，徒剧瞻向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234568_comment'></div>偶自正月感瘴，已七十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234568_comment'></div>迩来不能进食，加之呕吐，裹骨之具，亦已营治，无再晤之日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234568_comment'></div>床前授语子弟，为此不能周尽，然令兄书中可以互见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1234568_comment'></div>未间，万万惠时珍爱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1234568_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1234569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1234569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1234569?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答袁教授</a><span class='authorDate'>（1154年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33190, "宋", "郑刚中", "poem_title_1234569")'>郑刚中</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1234569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1234569'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1234569'>戊午兰省虽有得士之庆，然俾贤者志目中眉，亦有同愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1234569_comment'></div>阔别弥年，继以流落，杳不闻宦游所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1234569_comment'></div>自吕少卫忧去，始闻以绛帐犹与少卫为代，密迩相望，负戾不敢通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1234569_comment'></div>凡怀向之心，莫得自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1234569_comment'></div>专书下逮，情辞蔚然，佩荷之馀，如见天竺波澜也，益以钦仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1234569_comment'></div>某衰敝日甚，自正月二日感寒热，至今未平，骨立肉销，去死无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1234569_comment'></div>占语授甥孙辈书之，不能亲染。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1234569_comment'></div>尔后遇便，尚得别记，伏冀谅察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1234569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年5月23日</a>　夏，感疾，以其生之日月，终于封州，享年六十有七。<br /></div>
